World Peace Movement Congress Opens; More Than 3,000 Representatives from 40 Countries Attend; Our Representative Speaks, Willing to Strive for Peace; Congress Resolves to Ask Related Countries to Mediate the Spanish Civil War

Brussels: The International Peace Congress opened here today, with 3,000 representatives from 40 countries participating. A resolution was immediately passed asking the governments of countries related to the Spanish neutrality agreement to mediate the civil war in Spain. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

Brussels: The World Peace Movement Congress officially opened here last night at 8:00 PM. A total of more than 4,000 representatives from 37 countries attended. Lord Cecil, the chief representative of Britain, first welcomed the representatives of various countries. Mr. Guy La Chambre, the chief representative of France, the Minister of Aviation, then followed with a speech, stating that various countries have initiated peace movements to help the League of Nations and maintain peace. The task of this congress is to integrate these movements to concentrate forces. At this time, the Spanish representative Alvarez saluted with a fist according to the protocol of the Popular Front, and the audience immediately cheered enthusiastically. Most of the representatives also raised their fists in reply. Finally, Mr. Herriot, Speaker of the French Chamber of Deputies, gave a speech defending the three issues of military industrial nationalization, collective security, and mutual assistance conventions, and the discussion was lively, captivating the entire audience. (4th Havas Dispatch)

Brussels: The World Peace Movement Congress has officially opened here. The Chinese delegation includes the famous playwright Mr. Xiong Shiyi, who is famous in London for writing and directing the play "Wang Baochuan." At the opening of the congress this month, Mr. Wang Lixi, representative of the Chinese Students' Association in London, gave a speech on behalf of the Chinese delegation, stating that since September 18, China's national crisis has been serious and unprecedented, with internal and external troubles coming one after another. The people of our country have always had a spirit of peace. For the current plan, it is appropriate to organize and unite to participate in a wide-ranging peace movement, etc. (3rd Havas Dispatch)

Russian Delegation Arrives in Paris

(Paris) A delegation from the Moscow Soviet has arrived in Paris. The purpose of the delegation is to visit and study public buildings in major European cities. The leader of the delegation is Mr. Bulgannin, Chairman of the Moscow Soviet. (3rd Tass Dispatch)

The Western Rebel Army Advances Like a Bamboo Split; Y伦 City is Captured; The Champion Fights Bravely but Ultimately Succumbs; San Sebastian is Also Feared Difficult to Hold for Long

Piaabi - Spanish rebel forces captured Y伦 City today, immediately using knives and hand grenades to attack the defending forces. Fierce street fighting broke out, and the defenders surrendered due to lack of support. Thus, another important town in northern Spain has fallen. With the loss of this city, the wealthy port of San Sebastian is left with no defensible position, and the Spanish government forces' northwestern sea route is about to be cut off. (National Telegram, 4th)

Andaye - The northeastern fortress of Y伦 City, belonging to the Spanish government forces, was besieged by rebel forces for two weeks, followed by three days of intense fighting, resulting in hundreds of casualties on both sides. It was finally captured by the rebel forces today. At noon, the attacking rebel forces reached the center of the city. The main road leading to the border is still passable, allowing the remaining government forces to retreat. The defenders in the city have only a few machine gunners left, relying solely on the already burning houses as their only means of defense, and have vowed to fight to the death rather than flee or surrender. The rebel forces advanced in the city, using tanks and armored vehicles for cover. It is said that the rebel forces fought hard to capture the village of Beobia last night in order to remove the last obstacle to attacking Y伦. Although the defenders fiercely resisted with machine guns and rifles fired from the windows of houses along the way, the rebel forces fearlessly advanced step by step through the hail of bullets. The attacking rebel forces used Moroccan troops and foreign legions as their vanguard. While the government forces in the village of Beobia were desperately resisting, another rebel column bypassed the village and attacked Y伦. Subsequently, the defenders of Beobia finally collapsed and retreated, and the entire village was occupied by the rebel forces. Now that Y伦 City has fallen, San Sebastian is feared to be difficult to defend for long. It is said that the rebel forces are planning to begin an offensive. San Sebastian was originally a famous summer resort in Spain. Now, its land transportation has been cut off, and it is constantly subjected to aerial bombardment, transforming it into a terrifying hell. Several rebel warships are currently patrolling the coastal area of San Sebastian, preparing to open fire to provide assistance when the land offensive begins. If San Sebastian falls, the rebel forces can concentrate in the coastal cities west of the city, which are still held by government forces. Santander and Bilbao are also among them, as most of the country's military material factories are located within this region, making its gain or loss extremely significant. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

Andaye City, Southern France - Special dispatch from our correspondent: The Northern National Army of Spain has recently occupied Y伦. Under the cover of tanks and machine guns, the National Army advanced to the central area of the city at 9:00 this morning. Many houses were hit by bullets and caught fire, with flames raging throughout the city, making it impossible to approach. The complete fall of Y伦 City is imminent. The National Army made preparations last night and launched an attack along the Saint Martial to Y伦 City Avenue at dawn today. Their military equipment is far superior to that of the government forces, and they are advancing steadily, like a bamboo split. At the same time, another team rushed down from a high point near Y伦 City. The government forces were attacked from both sides, making them even more unable to withstand the assault. However, many members of the militia are brave individuals who had previously sworn to fight to the death. Although defeated, they are only willing to sacrifice themselves.

As for Beobia, another small town in the north, it is also surrounded by the National Army. Although the sound of gunfire has not ceased, the National Army has likely already controlled the town. Several hundred residents of Y伦 City have fled to this place since 6:00 this morning, gathering near the train station. Among them, soldiers belonging to the regular army and the militia are wearing blue workers' uniforms, covered in mud, and mostly looking dejected, without a single smile. As for the residents of the war zone, thousands have sought refuge in France in recent days. When leaving, they try to carry as many essential household items as possible. Those who are too heavy to carry are destroyed to prevent them from falling into the hands of the enemy. Many children have been separated from their families in the displacement, wandering the streets, crying out for their parents. Parents are also searching for their children everywhere, making it heart-wrenching to hear. Coupled with the bad weather, with fine rain, the scene is even more tragic. The fighting around Y伦 City has ended. Although the port of San Sebastian and the ports along the Atlantic coast are still in the hands of the government forces, they have been isolated from the French border, and their situation is also precarious. Furthermore, according to a special dispatch from our correspondent in Burgos City, the Northern Command of the National Army has now drafted a plan to prepare for an offensive against the ports of San Sebastian and Bilbao, and troops will likely be deployed at any moment. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Andaye City - Special dispatch from our correspondent: Street fighting broke out in Y伦 City, northern Spain, at 10:00 this morning. Although the militia belonging to the government forces are still desperately defending the city's outposts, the outposts in the town of Beobia have been occupied by the fascist Carlist party troops. Our correspondent personally witnessed dozens of militiamen stacking mattresses to form obstacles, using two machine guns to strafe the foreign legion and Moroccan soldiers belonging to the National Army. However, from the banks of the Bidasoa River on the border to the outskirts of Y伦 City, all areas are filled with National Army troops. Many of the government forces are hiding in civilian houses, constantly opening fire to hinder their advance. At this time, many houses in the city have been hit by bullets and are burning, with thick smoke rising everywhere. In addition, our correspondent also witnessed a militiaman fearlessly tearing down the Republican flag hanging high on the roof of the Y伦 City Hall, rolling it around the flagpole, and holding it tightly to his chest, showing his unwillingness to let it fall into the hands of the National Army. It can be said that their resentment is intense. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Great Chaos in Y伦; Fires Light Up the City; Refugees Flee to France in Despair; The Scene of Families Separated is Tragic

Andaye - This afternoon, a total of ten houses in Y伦 City caught fire and burned. When the burning buildings collapsed, large amounts of debris flew into the air, and the towering church spires were also heavily burned. The entire valley was shrouded in black smoke. After the rebel forces entered Y伦 City, fierce street fighting resumed because a small part of the government militia was still holding out. It was very clear from the border. The militia placed machine guns behind sandbags and launched a fierce strafing attack on the attacking foreign legion. Another thirty government soldiers hid behind another obstacle and fought bravely against the enemy. It is said that there are many houses in the city with explosives buried in them, all of which were detonated when the rebel forces entered the city. According to unconfirmed news, the government forces executed many hostages using high-voltage wires before withdrawing. It is said that Bishop Della Torre also suffered this fate. Traffic between Y伦 and San Sebastian was interrupted in the afternoon. Many of the defenders are still holding out near the international bridge, using machine guns to strafe the enemy. The rebel forces occupied the city hall during the fighting. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

The refugees who fled from Y伦 to the French border today were in a very miserable state, carrying as many of their belongings as possible. There were two young girls carrying a birdcage, which still contained a hibiscus bird. The weather was unfavorable, with incessant overcast rain, which made the refugees even more miserable and sick. When passing through the border, many children were separated from their parents and were crying sadly. Many refugees had too much clutter at home to carry conveniently, and many destroyed it themselves, preferring to sacrifice everything rather than have it used by the rebel forces. The French authorities are now distributing all the refugees to various towns and cities in southern France. Currently, Andaye alone has gathered more than 5,000 refugees, many of whom swam across the Bidasoa River to France under the hail of bullets. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

Rebel Forces Exert All Their Strength to Attack the City of Beobia; With the Loss of This Barrier, Y伦 is Difficult to Defend

Andaye - This afternoon, the Spanish rebel forces began to attack the city of Beobia on the Spanish-French border. Without taking this city, there is no hope of capturing Y伦 City. At 4:45 p.m., 1,500 infantrymen from the rebel side launched their first fierce attack on the city from the slopes of Mount Labencia, with Moroccan troops and foreign legions as the vanguard. As the foreign legions advanced, they threw grenades along the way. The defenders resisted with machine guns, with bullets raining down. After about fifteen minutes, the rebel forces finally reached the outskirts of the city, but many of their leaders were killed. Because the defenders were mostly hiding in houses, firing fiercely from the windows, while the attacking troops had no cover when they rushed forward, they only relied on their large numbers to advance quickly to reach their destination. At dusk, the fighting became even more intense. Everything along the avenue along the Bidasoa River was swept away by fierce artillery fire. The defenders crouched behind obstacles and sandbags, using machine guns and rifles to fire at the foreign legions who were trying to occupy the bridgehead over the river. Late tonight, the rebel forces, using the power of machine guns, advanced to a location within 400 yards of the international bridge. In addition to braving the hail of bullets from the government forces' machine guns, they were also subjected to continuous rifle fire from the upper-story windows of the houses. Then, the rebel artillery began to shell the unoccupied parts of Beobia, causing two shells to land on the tracks near the Andaye train station, but they did not explode. However, one shell hit a match factory, which burned fiercely in an instant. Another stray bullet cut the city's electricity wires, plunging the entire city of Beobia into darkness. The sound of bullets whistling through the air was incessant on the avenue within the French border, causing local residents to close their windows tightly. At the same time, the sound of grenades exploding was also heard on the avenue connecting Y伦 and San Marcial. (Reuters Telegram, 3rd)

Town of Beobia on the Franco-Spanish Border - This afternoon, Spanish rebel artillery and aircraft fiercely bombarded Y伦 City and the Fontarabia Fortress, continuously causing tremendous losses. The sky was filled with smoke, covering the advance of the rebel forces. The troops, including Carlist restorationists and Moroccan foreign legions, were making slow but fierce progress. Armed combatants from the People's Front were desperately defending every inch of land, digging trenches in the fields to resist with rifles and machine guns, and would not give up until the very end. At the time of writing this dispatch by the Havas News Agency correspondent, bullets were flying through the streets of Beobia, France, with a whistling sound. The town of Beobia on the western side is still in the hands of the government forces, but it is in imminent danger of being captured by the rebel forces at any moment. At 8:30 p.m., sixty-six government soldiers crossed into French territory and were disarmed and accommodated. Looking through a telescope at dusk, our correspondent glimpsed the rebel demolition team throwing explosives at the last line of defense held by the government forces. The government forces fled through the wheat fields. The reporter personally witnessed one of them being slightly delayed in his escape, and his head was immediately blown off by the explosion. The horrifying scene of the battlefield can be seen from this. The rebel forces continued to advance without stopping. Beobia seems to be indefensible, but a few government soldiers are still putting up a last-ditch resistance. Many of the rebel rifles and machine gun bullets landed in France, causing great panic among the French people. Marcant, the prefect of the Lower Pyrenees province of France, has lodged a strong protest with the rebel headquarters in Danquierinea. It is reported that the rebel commander General Mola has promised to order his troops not to harm the safety of French territory. (Havas Telegram, 3rd)

Southwest Front: The Rebel Army Eyes the Capital, Launching a Fierce Attack on the Champion's Position; Part of the Army Penetrates the Outskirts of Malaga

Madrid - The battle for the rebel army to seize the western capital has been raging for the past four days. At 3:00 a.m. this morning, the rebel army resumed its fierce attack on the government army's position from the west. The government army has dispatched several columns of reinforcements and a number of aircraft in an attempt to cut off the rebel army's transportation line. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

Lisbon - According to news from Avila, a column of rebel troops commanded by Colonel Yagoda, advancing from Badajoz towards Toledo and Madrid, occupied Talavilla after a fierce battle last night. The government forces suffered heavy losses. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

Seville - General Deliano, commander of the Southern Andalusian Division of the National Army, recently issued a broadcast message stating that our army, advancing north from the province of Toledo, occupied the city of Talavera yesterday afternoon and is now only 117 kilometers away from the capital. In this battle, 400 officers and soldiers of the government army were killed, and four aircraft, ten cannons, many machine guns, and several trucks were seized. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Lisbon - The "Secular Newspaper" published a report today based on a report from its Seville correspondent, stating that Spanish rebel forces have penetrated the outskirts of Malaga. It is said that the rebel leader General Lano has informed the right-wing leader Vanlela of this news. Some of the civilians in Malaga are preparing to surrender due to the renewed bombing by the rebel forces. Currently, the rebel aircraft's bombing target is one of the nearby government army airfields. (National Telegram, 3rd)

(Paris) - The Spanish ambassador to France recently sent a note from his government to Foreign Minister Delbos, stating that nearly twenty-four Italian-made aircraft arrived in the port of Vigo this morning for use by the rebel army, which clearly violates the non-intervention agreement. Spanish Territorial Waters - Italy Increases Naval Strength; Another Italian National is Killed; A Serious Protest is Lodged

(Rome) - A government spokesman announced today that Italy has increased its naval strength in Spanish territorial waters because an Italian national was killed in Spain this week. According to reports, the murdered person's name is Fassarella, a plumber in Barcelona. Official reports have been received here today stating that the only reason for his murder was that religious paintings were found in his home. The Italian consul in Barcelona has been ordered to lodge a serious protest with the Catalan government. (National Telegram, 3rd)

(Rome) - According to news from the port of Barcelona, Spain, an Italian national was killed there yesterday. This is the sixth Italian national to have been killed since the outbreak of the civil unrest in Spain. People here were shocked by the news. The deceased national, surnamed Fassarella, worked as a plumber and had seven children. It is said that the reason for his death was that he possessed religious books and images, which angered the left-wing People's Front party members. However, the details of what happened are currently unknown. The Italian consul in the port of Barcelona has lodged a strong protest with the local authorities regarding this matter. An official announcement stated that "Under the current circumstances, such a protest is of no avail." The government has dispatched the 10,000-ton cruiser "Pola" to the port of Barcelona. It should be noted that after the previous case of an Italian national being killed in the area, the Italian light cruiser "Adantoro" has been stationed there and is still docked in the port. (Havas Telegram, 3rd)

Italian Embassy Moves to Alicante

(Rome) - Because the Madrid government cannot guarantee safety, Italy is following in Germany's footsteps and moving its embassy to Alicante. It is said that this decision is unrelated to the case of the Italian national being killed in Barcelona, and the Italian government currently has no intention of demanding compensation, as it is useless to conduct any negotiations with the Madrid government, which is in a state of "loss of power." The United States Decides to Follow the British Example, Retaining 40,000 Tons of Destroyers; Japanese Note Delivered to Washington

(Washington) - In July, the British government notified both Japan and the United States, stating that the British government had decided to invoke Article 21 of the 1930 London Naval Treaty, the "escalator clause," to maintain a total destroyer tonnage of 190,000 tons (the London Treaty originally stipulated 150,000 tons). In other words, it would retain the 40,000 tons of old ships that should have been dismantled this year according to the treaty. US Secretary of State Hull has officially announced that the United States intends to follow the British example and retain 40,000 tons of destroyers that exceed the age limit and should be dismantled according to the London Treaty. (Havas Telegram, 3rd)

(Washington) - Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito recently delivered a note to Secretary of State Hull, stating that since the British government has requested to retain 40,000 tons of destroyers that should have been dismantled according to the London Treaty, the Japanese government also requests that 2,059 tons of destroyers and 15,598 tons of submarines that have reached their service age be retained as well. US naval officials have long known that Japan has fewer destroyers that have reached their age limit and that it is insufficient to retain them according to the example. Therefore, they do not find it strange that the country has also requested to retain submarine tonnage to compensate for this. As for the United States, the United States has many destroyers that have reached their age limit, and it is not difficult to retain 40,000 tons according to the example. There are also submarines that have reached their age limit, which can be retained as well. Therefore, the United States does not worry about not being able to cope with Japan's move to increase its naval tonnage. However, the US government has now decided to follow the British example and retain 40,000 tons of destroyers that should be dismantled according to the London Treaty. This point has been confirmed by Secretary of State Hull, but no decision has yet been made on how to handle the submarine tonnage. All naval experts advocate retaining submarines that have reached their age limit at the same time, because the current naval treaties will expire at the end of this year. If the US Congress can approve the new naval treaty signed by the United Kingdom, the United States and France in London this year, then the naval tonnage restrictions will no longer exist from January 1 of next year, and the old submarine tonnage can be fully retained. (According to the new naval treaty signed by the United Kingdom, the United States and France this year, only qualitative restrictions are included.) (Havas Telegram, 3rd)

Japan Requests to Retain Submarines - The Opinion of the British Naval Community

(London) - People in the British naval community are discussing this decision by Japan and have very different opinions. Strictly speaking, the London Naval Treaty only allows Japan to retain warships of the same type as those retained by the United Kingdom. However, the Japanese side argues that its navy has very few destroyers that are too old, which is quite different from the 28,000 tons permitted in the treaty, so submarines are used to make up for the difference. British naval experts all believe that Japan's existing submarines have already reached the maximum tonnage permitted in the treaty. If it wants to retain them now, then its quantity will greatly exceed the limit by the end of this year. It is also heard that the United States is unlikely to object, because Japan's actions do not violate the spirit of the treaty, and it is much more economical to retain old submarines than to build new destroyers, as the treaty will soon expire. (Reuters Telegram, 3rd)

United States Plans to Strengthen the Merchant Fleet by Adding 350 Ships

(Washington) - The US Department of Commerce's Shipping Bureau is now preparing to submit a report on the national shipping policy to the newly established Maritime Commission. Officials from the Shipping Bureau vigorously advocated the necessity of strengthening the merchant fleet on the 3rd, saying that most of the US merchant ships are old and do not meet modern requirements. Therefore, it seems that in order to reach the standards of other countries, it is necessary to build 350 new ships. The Maritime Commission will use 500 million US dollars in shipping subsidies this year to start implementing the plan to build new ships, but the cooperation of the private sector is essential to strengthening and expanding the merchant fleet. (Allied News Agency Telegram, 3rd)

Frequent Border Disputes: Russia Rejects Japanese Protest, Blaming Japan for the Dongning Incident and Demanding a Joint Committee for Resolution

(Moscow) Yesterday, the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires in the Soviet Union visited Mr. Kazlovsky, the Soviet Russian Minister for the Far East, to protest the so-called violation of the border by Soviet border troops in Dongning, and the illegal firing incident. According to the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires, on August 28th, eight bullets from the Soviet territory fell into the "Manchurian" territory in Dongning. On the same day and at the same location, a Soviet machine gun fired upon the Japanese border troops in Shilongtun, resulting in one "Manchurian" injury. On the same day and at the same location, a Soviet aircraft intruded into "Manchurian" territory.

Mr. Kazlovsky has firmly rejected the Japanese protest, stating that he himself protested to the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires on August 27th regarding the incident of Japanese and "Manchurian" soldiers bombarding Soviet border troops watering their horses within Soviet territory, and demanded an immediate thorough investigation and punishment. Mr. Kazlovsky asked the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires to note that when the Japanese side raised a counter-protest on August 29th, claiming that the incident occurred in "Manchurian" territory, and that a Soviet border troop's corpse was left within "Manchurian" territory, Mr. Litvinov had firmly rejected the protest, saying it was based on completely false reports, and specifically pointed out the fabrication of abandoning a Red Army soldier's corpse within "Manchurian" territory. At the same time, he reiterated a firm protest against the illegal actions of the Japanese and "Manchurian" sides, which deliberately sought to provoke border conflicts.

Mr. Kazlovsky pointed out that, based on extremely accurate and verified records, he could firmly state that the Japanese report regarding the Soviet border troops' alleged violation of the border near Dongning on August 28th was completely fabricated. Mr. Kazlovsky asked the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires to note the recent incident on August 31st of Japanese and "Manchurian" troops bombarding Soviet border troops. Mr. Kazlovsky said, "The constant fabrication of news by the Japanese authorities in Manchuria, and the attempt to shift the responsibility for creating a serious situation onto the Soviet Union, gives the impression that a certain segment of the Japanese military stationed in Manchuria is attempting to pre-emptively conceal their prepared new provocations and make them appear justified. The Soviet government asks the Japanese government to pay special attention to this point and declares that the Japanese side should bear full responsibility."

The Soviet government believes that the continued existence of the current border situation is intolerable and endangers peace. Therefore, it suggests immediately forming a joint Soviet-Japanese-"Manchurian" committee, which the Japanese government formally agreed to on February 14th, but its actual organization has been delayed due to the Japanese side's fault. This committee should be authorized to thoroughly investigate all recent similar incidents. Mr. Kazlovsky finally asked the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires to note the recent incidents of Japanese and "Manchurian" troops invading the Soviet border in various places along the Soviet-"Manchurian" border. The Soviet government has instructed its ambassador in Tokyo to lodge a protest. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

Japan Actively Prepares for War: Expanding Aviation Education, Requiring an Expenditure of Four Million Yuan

(Tokyo) Japanese Minister of the Army, General Terauchi, in view of the fact that all countries in the world are devoting their full efforts to the development of aviation, seeking to strengthen national defense capabilities, especially with the rapid progress of the Soviet Union, keenly felt the necessity for Japan's aviation industry to catch up, thereby solidifying national defense. He decided to start expanding aviation education in the next year's budget, estimated to require an expenditure of approximately four million yuan, which will be added to the next year's new budget, and requested the approval of the Ministry of Finance. The preliminary content is outlined as follows: (1) Increase the budget by 200,000 yuan to expand the Department of Aeronautics in the Faculty of Engineering at Tokyo Imperial University. (2) Establish new Departments of Aeronautics at Osaka and Kyushu Imperial Universities, with 580,000 yuan allocated to equip the two universities. Starting in the 13th year of the Republic (1924), outstanding young people will be recruited and subjected to rigorous training. (3) Establish new Departments of Aeronautics at Yokohama, Nagoya, Hamamatsu, and Hiroshima Higher Industrial Schools, starting next year, with over 600,000 yuan allocated. All courses at these schools will focus on combat academics, aiming to cultivate civil aviation talents in preparation for future wars. (4) (Hualian dispatch, 4th)

Germany Suggests to Lithuania Concluding a Non-Aggression Pact, Negotiations with Baltic Coastal States Will Also Commence Soon

Germans Unforgettable: Recovering Old Colonies, Leading Figures of the National Socialist Party Publish Papers Saying There Is Full Legal Basis

(Berlin) Governor of Bavaria and Chief of the Colonial Policy Office of the National Socialist Party, Chairman of the German Colonial Union, General Epp, recently published an article in the "European Review" magazine on the issue of Germany's demand for colonies. He stated that Germany's demand for the return of colonies is limited to the pre-war colonies deprived by the Treaty of Versailles. The reasons held by General Epp for Germany's demand for colonies are as follows: (1) The territory under German jurisdiction is too narrow to accommodate its population. (2) The existing German territory does not produce various major raw materials. (3) After the colonies were deprived, Germany was relegated to a second-class country. General Epp also said, "The purpose of the German colonial movement is only to abolish the principle that Germany cannot possess colonies and to restore the right of national self-determination in various colonies. It is most unfair not to allow Germany to possess colonies and contradicts the treaty on the Congo signed by the powers in 1885. According to Article 11 of that treaty, the powers solemnly guaranteed that if a war occurred in Europe, it would not involve the colonies. However, it was not Germany that subsequently violated the Congo Treaty, as a British cruiser first opened fire on German East Africa on August 5, 1914, after the outbreak of the Great War. Furthermore, during the Great War, U.S. President Wilson announced fourteen points for peace negotiations, the fifth of which stipulated that the colonial issue should be decided by international arbitration. Later, Article 159 of the Treaty of Versailles regarding German colonies contradicted that fifth point. Moreover, the value of the colonies lost by Germany after the war was not included in Germany's indemnity payments. Therefore, Germany's demand to restore its pre-war colonies has an absolutely sufficient legal basis." (Havas dispatch, 3rd)

Regarding the first point, the production quantity of various military factories should be increased, and workers' strikes should be prevented. Britain Increases Troops to Palestine, Sussex Autumn Maneuvers Cancelled, British Garrison in Fierce Battle with Arabs

(London) The large maneuvers of the First Infantry Division in Sussex were canceled yesterday, indicating that the British government will send more troops to Palestine. It is reported that the current British garrison in Palestine consists of about ten battalions. If martial law is implemented, it will not be enough to curb the riots. The Morning Post stated that political circles view the cancellation of the maneuvers as sufficient to indicate that unless the Arabs in Palestine stop the strike and all acts of violence, the British authorities intend to declare martial law. It is now believed that the British authorities have given the Arab Higher Committee sufficient warning and have informed them that the government is prepared to do its utmost to assist in persuading the Arabs. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Jerusalem: Today, the British troops stationed in Palestine engaged in fierce fighting with the Arabs all day in the area of Tulkarm, north of Jerusalem. As a result, three British soldiers were killed and four were wounded. On the Arab side, ten were killed, and the casualties from the air force bombing have not yet been counted. Among the British dead were the pilot, Air Force officer Hunter, and the machine gunner on the plane, who died on the spot when their plane crashed at the foot of a small hill during combat. Among the wounded was the pilot of another plane, who, although wounded in the leg by a bullet, was able to safely land the plane, and an army officer and two soldiers. Today's battle can be described as the most serious since the disturbances in Palestine. The battle began in the morning, when the British Lincoln and Scottish Regiments, in cooperation with the Air Force, encountered a group of over fifty Arabs south of Tulkarm and immediately opened fire. Many of the Arabs fired from the mountainside, but were eventually defeated and retreated to the village of Balai. Later, the Air Force arrived and continued to pursue, and the number of Arab casualties was quite high. However, the Arabs still tried to resist on land, so a British sergeant was killed on the spot, and one officer and two soldiers were wounded. At the same time, it was rumored that the British High Commissioner for Palestine, Sir Arthur Wauchope, had agreed that if the disturbances ceased, the immigration of Jews would be stopped. This statement has been denied in a letter by the British Colonial Secretary, Mr. Gore. (Reuters dispatch, 3rd)

Legislative Yuan Passes County Autonomy Law, Dispute Assessment Committee is Deemed Unnecessary

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 70th meeting on the morning of the 4th, with 56 members including Lin Bin present. Sun Ke presided as chairman, and Liang Hanchao as secretary-general. Matters discussed: (1) The Autonomy Law Committee reported on the revised draft of the County Autonomy Law, and it was resolved to pass the revision. (2) The Legislative Committee reported on the examination of the Organizational Law of the Authority Dispute Assessment Committee, and it was resolved that the committee was not necessary. The main reasons were: A. To maintain the independence and integrity of the Judicial Yuan's judgment and interpretation powers, there is no need to establish the committee. Even if the committee is organized with the existing staff of the Executive and Judicial Yuans, it would be difficult to obtain fair results in assessing disputes between the two Yuans regarding their own powers. B. Since an assessment committee must be established to resolve disputes between the Executive and Judicial Yuans, disputes over authority also occur between the other two of the five Yuans. In the future, there will inevitably be requests to establish similar committees, which will further complicate government agencies. C. Regarding matters that cannot be resolved between the Yuans, Article 17 of the National Government Organization Law already clearly stipulates a method of resolution. Based on the above reasons, the proposal was rejected, and President Sun instructed the Legislative Committee to organize the above reasons in writing for review by the Central Political Council. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

(Nanjing) Huang Youchang, the convener of the Autonomy Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan, reported on the review process of the preliminary report on the revision of the County Autonomy Law at the Yuan meeting on the 4th, stating briefly: After receiving the eight principles of local autonomy laws and regulations issued by the Central Government, a meeting was convened. First, the County Autonomy Law passed by the 86th meeting of the Third Session of this Yuan was submitted for discussion. Based on the central principles and other laws, Articles 2, 3, 43, 44, 53, 59, and 73 of the law were revised, and the original Article 74 was deleted and a new Article 75 was added. In addition, Principle 4 issued by the Central Government states that county governments may, due to geographical, demographic, economic, cultural, and other special circumstances, submit applications to higher-level agencies for approval to establish districts to guide autonomous affairs. There was a general agreement to stipulate this in the Implementing Rules of the County Autonomy Law. As for the autonomous self-defense funds and personnel, they cannot be separated. Based on the results of my inspection of the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Hunan, the Baojia system is incorporated into the autonomous organization, which is already a reality today. However, the organization and implementation of the Baojia system produced by the County Autonomy Law cannot be stipulated in the County Autonomy Law and must be separately stipulated in the Baojia Regulations. Because the Autonomy Law cannot be easily changed, the Baojia Regulations can be changed with the evolution of the autonomous period and the development of civil rights. Therefore, Article 75 has been added. A total of eight articles of the County Autonomy Law amendment have been opened, and the rest have not been modified. The Implementing Rules of the County Autonomy Law, the City Autonomy Law, and its Implementing Rules, and the Baojia Regulations are currently being reviewed in meetings and will be reported to the meeting for further consideration as soon as they are completed. After finishing the speech, Chen Changheng objected to the provision in Article 74 of the amendment, which stipulates that men and women aged 20 or older who reside in this Baojia shall be residents of this Baojia, stating that according to the interpretation of the text of this article, men and women under the age of 20 no longer have resident status, which is unfair in legislation. He advocated deleting the article, which was unanimously passed. The other revised articles were also slightly questioned by the committee members, but all were passed according to the amendment. According to the original County Autonomy Law, which was passed by the 86th meeting of the Third Session of the Yuan on December 21, 1934, there are nine chapters, including Autonomous Regions, County Autonomous Matters, County Citizens, County People's Congress, County Council, County Government, County Finance, Townships and Districts, and Supplementary Provisions, totaling 77 articles, as reported by the Pazhi at the time, but has not been officially promulgated by the National Government. The number of chapters passed by the revised meeting on the 4th remains the same. The articles have been reduced by two compared to the original draft, and a new Article 1 has been added, totaling 76 articles. The main points of the revision are: (1) Incorporate the Baojia system into the autonomous organization. The organization below the county level is one level. The original neighborhoods in the townships are abolished and changed to Baojia. Ten neighborhoods make up a Jia, with a Jia head. Ten Jia make up a Bao, with a Bao head. Ten or more Bao make up a township or district. However, the division and organization of townships and districts may be adjusted according to local natural conditions or customs. The county seat may be divided into several districts, which are at the same level as the townships and districts, and their organization is the same. (2) The County Defense Corps Law is abolished to avoid duplication with the Baojia system. The Baojia Regulations are stipulated separately. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

League of Nations Releases World Trade Yearbook

(London) According to the League of Nations Yearbook, the stability of exchange rates in 1935 caused the gold price of world trade to increase slightly by 1.9%, which is the first time since 1929. If calculated in British gold pounds, the increase is about 5.3%. Currently, the gold price of European trade has fallen by 2%, while the combined trade of other continents has increased by 6%, with North America benefiting the most. US imports increased by 24% and exports increased by 6.2%. The exports of countries in the Gold Bloc have all declined, with France's figures decreasing by 13.5%, the Netherlands by 5%, and the Dutch East Indies by 4.5%. However, the trade of the following countries has all trended upwards: Germany increased by 4.2%, China increased by 13.5%, Japan increased by 10.8%, the United Kingdom increased by 4.6%, India increased by 3%, Malaya increased by 1%, and South Africa increased by 24%. The above percentages are all compared with 1934. (3rd, Reuters)

British Naval, Land, and Air Forces Conduct Exercises in Singapore to Test Defenses of Pulau Blakang Mati

During the exercises, ship traffic was temporarily prohibited from passing through the western entrance of the port. The artillery garrison on the island also participated in the exercises. Educational Broadcasting Supplement

The Food Self-Sufficiency Problem in Extraordinary Times (Part 1)

— Tong Runzhi, Head of the Agricultural Department of Jiangsu Educational Institute

(1) The Importance of Food Self-Sufficiency in Extraordinary Times

Food self-sufficiency is a very important issue in extraordinary times. The reason Germany lost in the European War and the Allied Powers won was primarily due to this point. During this period, the entire nation must pay attention to the issue of food production and food conservation. However, this task is too significant and can only be effective if the government formulates policies to control food production, consumption, and distribution. Moreover, many tasks, such as land distribution, wasteland utilization, food price regulation, and prevention of merchant monopolies, cannot succeed without the government using political power to control them. However, government control policies are difficult to implement smoothly without the support of the people. During the European War, the implementation of food control policies in England, America, Germany, and France was relatively successful, largely because the general public already had training; however, social unrest still occurred. Germany failed because of food shortages, and the United States would have had difficulty winning if it were not blessed with abundant production. As for our Chinese people, who have always lacked education, once war breaks out, various phenomena of disintegration, upheaval, and disorder will inevitably arise. Maintaining law and order has already become a major problem, let alone food control! This requires large-scale and extremely effective public education to guide them on how to work hard to increase production, transport and sell products, and control consumption under government control. If farmers can calmly engage in production and ensure that there are no concerns about food supply, then the war can be won. Therefore, public education is necessary in extraordinary times, and public education must pay attention to this issue of food self-sufficiency.

(2) The Current Status of Food Self-Sufficiency in Our Country and Speculations After the Outbreak of War

Can our country be self-sufficient in food during normal times? The answer to this question must be analyzed based on our country's peacetime food production, consumption, and international trade. Our main food crops are rice, wheat, and miscellaneous grains. According to the estimation of the Central Agricultural Experiment Station, the average annual output of various food crops in the recent three years (1933 to 1935) is approximately 1.8 billion shi, of which 800 million shi are rice and 450 million shi are wheat. In terms of quantity, our country can be considered the world's largest rice and wheat producer. However, although production is high, consumption is also large. Although there are no precise statistics on annual consumption, it can be seen from the annual excess of rice and wheat imports that our rice and wheat production is not yet self-sufficient. Rice has always been insufficient for consumption, and imports of foreign rice have been increasing year by year. In 1912, it was 2.7 million shi; in 1922, it increased to more than 19 million shi; and in 1932, it further increased to 23 million shi, while the annual export volume is very small. Before 1923, wheat was not only self-sufficient but also had an annual surplus for export. However, since 1924, except for a small surplus in 1927, all other years have been years of import surplus. In recent years, the annual import volume has generally been around 20 million shi. Furthermore, according to the latest report from the Customs, the total value of rice imports in 1935 was 93 million yuan, an increase of 42% compared to 1934; the total value of wheat imports was 36 million yuan, an increase of 14% compared to the previous year. The combined total for rice and wheat is 120 million yuan, which shows that domestic rice and wheat production cannot be self-sufficient, and the degree of deficiency is deepening year by year. In addition, miscellaneous grains and miscellaneous grain flour were originally self-sufficient. Before 1932, the export surplus was very large, but most of it was produced in the Northeast and exported from Northeast ports. However, since the September 18th Incident, there have been almost no reports of miscellaneous grain exports in the Customs trade records, indicating that miscellaneous grain self-sufficiency has also become a problem in recent years. In summary, from all perspectives, our country's food supply is insufficient for consumption, and the quantity lacking is increasing year by year.

Although rice and wheat are imported annually, the imported quantity is very low compared to the total consumption. Assuming that the number of rice eaters accounts for half of the country's population and each person's annual consumption is 2 shi, then the total annual consumption is approximately 500 million shi, and the daily consumption is approximately 1.3 million shi. Therefore, the annual import of 20 million shi of foreign rice only supplies the national rice-eating population with food for two weeks, and the quantity lacking cannot be considered large. Japan's annual rice import surplus accounts for 14% of total consumption, which is a much higher degree of rice deficiency than our country. Regarding wheat, although there is an annual import surplus, the imported quantity only accounts for 1% of the total consumption. If there were no wheat and flour imports, the quantity of wheat lacking would only be enough for ten days. Therefore, some people say that although our country's food cannot be completely self-sufficient, it is very close to self-sufficiency. As long as production increases slightly, there will be no concerns about food. However, this statement is correct when viewed from the perspective of normal times. In extraordinary times, the situation is different. Countries that can be self-sufficient in food during normal times often cannot be self-sufficient during wartime. If food cannot be self-sufficient during peacetime, it can still be remedied; however, if food cannot be self-sufficient during wartime, the danger is extremely great. Assuming that we do not pay attention to this food problem now, then once wartime arrives, the following unfortunate phenomena will inevitably occur:

(1) Reduced cultivated land and increased wasteland This is because (1) a portion of young and strong farmers directly or indirectly participate in military work and cannot engage in cultivation; (2) cultivation in or near war zones is inconvenient, or even if planted, it cannot be harvested; (3) farmers fear war and flee, resulting in abandoned fields; (4) farmers with bad habits take the opportunity to abandon their original occupations and engage in improper activities; (5) a portion of cultivated land is occupied by the enemy, and agricultural products are no longer owned by us, as is the case in the four northeastern provinces.

(2) Reduced food supply and increased prices This is because (1) since cultivated land is reduced, production also decreases accordingly; (2) transportation is inconvenient, not only is it difficult to import foreign rice, but even the transportation of domestic rice and wheat is more difficult than in normal times; (3) unscrupulous merchants monopolize the market and hoard food, leading to high prices; (4) the general public competes to purchase food for unexpected needs, and the market supply gradually decreases; (5) people's appetite increases during wartime, making the food supply even more insufficient.

(3) Disrupted social order and greatly affected military affairs This is because (1) food shortages lead to widespread panic; (2) traitors rise up, making it impossible to stabilize the rear, and most people only know how to escape and seek refuge, not how to defend themselves; (3) insufficient rations make it impossible to maintain military discipline; (4) military forces are divided to defend the interior and cannot be concentrated for external defense.

The above three phenomena are all directly or indirectly caused by food shortages. To avoid these phenomena, preparations must be made early. These preparations certainly rely on the government to formulate and implement food control measures, but the efforts and preparations of the people themselves are especially important.

So, how should we, the general public, work hard and assist the government in solving this food self-sufficiency problem? I believe that we must work hard in three areas: first, strive to increase food production to reduce import surplus; second, promote and implement food conservation to reduce consumption; and third, calm the minds of farmers to maintain agricultural labor. If all three of these tasks are effective, then we will not fear food shortages in extraordinary times. Now let me explain them separately.

(3) How to Increase Food Production

There are many ways to increase food production. I will now only present four relatively important ones:

(1) Adopt improved rice and wheat varieties During extraordinary times, our rural compatriots engaged in food production should contact agricultural experiment and educational institutions more often to switch to improved rice and wheat varieties to increase food production. After years of breeding and experimentation, agricultural experiment and educational institutions across the country have cultivated many improved rice, wheat, and miscellaneous grain varieties that can be supplied to farmers in various regions. Approximately fifteen wheat varieties have been successfully improved and promoted, and more than a dozen varieties are being propagated for promotion. Even more varieties are in the experimental stage and have the potential for promotion. The average yield is more than 20% higher than that of local farmers' varieties. More than twenty rice varieties have been successfully improved and promoted, and they can increase the yield by an average of more than 10%. Among the improved miscellaneous grain varieties, there are thirteen millet varieties and eleven sorghum varieties. Others, such as soybeans and corn, are also being bred and have achieved good results. If our rural compatriots can select seeds themselves and maintain close contact with agricultural education or extension agencies in various regions, and adopt improved varieties and cultivation methods, I believe that the nation's food production can increase by 10% in five years.

After the Guangxi Army Entered Guangdong, Cargo Transport on the Southern Route of Guangdong Province Was Suspended; The Main Forces of the Guangxi Army Were Transferring to the Northeast of Guangxi; The Headquarters of the Guangxi Army Promulgated Wartime Reward and Punishment Regulations

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since the Guangxi Army's troops under Weng Zhaoyuan and others entered the southern district of Guangdong Province on the 25th, the Songjiang steamships traveling between Guangzhou and Leizhou have now been suspended. Ships departing from Guangzhou to Shuidong, Meicha, and other places have also been completely suspended. Merchants in the southern route here have stopped handling goods since the 29th. It is reported that Gaolei, Qinlian, and other areas south of Liangyang are now under the control of the Guangxi Army. It is also rumored that three regiments of the Guangxi Provincial Militia were found in Xinyi County, which borders Luoding. Therefore, the Southern District Pacification Office and various agencies in Meicha have mostly relocated. It has been found that the Guangxi Army stationed in the four prefectures of Gaolei, Qinlian, and others are all reorganized from the militia. The regular army of the Guangxi Army has not yet entered Guangdong and is still tightly guarding the Guangxi border. After the Guangxi province expanded its forces, Bai Chongxi and Cai Tingkai were appointed as the commanders-in-chief of the First and Second Route Armies, respectively. Each route army commands three columns. In the First Route Army, Liao Lei commands the First Column, Li Pinxian commands the Second Column, and Xia Wei commands the Third Column. In the Second Route Army, Weng Zhaoyuan commands the First Column, Qu Shounian commands the Second Column, and Shen Guanghan (replaced by Xie Bingxun) commands the Third Column. The two route armies are responsible for operations in Guilin, Liuzhou, Nanning, and Wuzhou. According to the current situation, the Guangxi Army seems to emphasize the northeast of Guangxi and adopts a defensive posture in the southwest of Guangxi. On the 20th of this month, the 7th Army of Liao Lei's troops moved from Liu to Guixian to reinforce the Yulin-Bobai line. The headquarters of the 7th Army is located in Guiping. The 15th Army of Xia Wei's troops, originally stationed in Guilin, also moved to Longhu Pass, Hexian, and Bapu. Guilin was then defended by the 8th Army of Li Pinxian's troops. Only a small number of troops were left on the Yunnan-Guizhou border to cooperate with the militia in defense. Currently, only the 21st Division of Biao Junchang's troops of the 7th Army is defending the Baise area on the Yunnan border. Only the 26th Division of Mo Shujie's troops of the 8th Army is stationed in Nandan, Hechi, and other places on the Guizhou border. However, the Guangxi Army has adopted a guerrilla strategy in this operation, and each army is not limited to stationed defenses to facilitate flexible deployment. The headquarters of the Guangxi Army has recently promulgated wartime reward and punishment regulations. The original text is as follows: Article 1. These regulations are specially formulated during the time of war to ensure the security of the war zone and to prevent any harm from the enemy, to punish reactionaries, and to reward meritorious people. Article 2. The term "war zone" mentioned in the preceding article shall be temporarily demarcated and announced by order of the General Headquarters of the Army's Headquarters, taking into consideration the circumstances. Article 3. Any citizen in the war zone who commits any of the following acts shall be sentenced to death: 1. Gathering people to resist orders or engaging in rioting; 2. Colluding with the enemy to plot to disrupt public order; 3. Acting as a scout for the enemy or assisting the enemy's scout; 4. Serving the enemy; 5. Acting as a guide or messenger for the enemy, or providing geographical information; 6. Recruiting troops for the enemy or joining the enemy army. Article 4. Any citizen in the war zone who helps the enemy to harm our army and commits any of the following acts shall be sentenced to death: 1. Supplying the enemy with military equipment, ammunition, food, or other important military supplies; 2. Destroying the army's military equipment, ammunition, food depots, or other important military supplies, or rendering them unusable by other means; 3. Leaking or delivering to the enemy information about the army's movements, secret documents, maps, and military intelligence; 4. Damaging the army's fortresses, military camps, military ships, aircraft, and other military buildings, or rendering them unusable by other means; 5. Damaging or blocking land and water bridges or hindering the army's transportation by other means; 6. Seizing or releasing captured ships or prisoners for the enemy. Article 5. Any citizen in the war zone who commits any of the following acts shall be sentenced to death, life imprisonment, or imprisonment for more than ten years: 1. Instigating soldiers to be disobedient or desert; 2. Spreading rumors to confuse the public or engaging in reactionary propaganda through speeches; 3. Destroying or hindering the army's "clear the fields" strategy. Article 6. Any citizen in the war zone who, in addition to the acts listed in Articles 3 to 5, engages in other significant acts of helping the enemy or harming the army shall be sentenced to imprisonment for one to ten years. Article 7. Any citizen in the war zone who has any of the following meritorious achievements shall be given a bonus ranging from five to one hundred yuan, depending on the circumstances: 1. Seizing enemy firearms, ammunition, or other important military supplies, in addition to being allowed to own them, shall be rewarded according to their nature and quantity; 2. Capturing or killing enemy officers shall be rewarded according to their rank; 3. Discovering important secret documents or information about the enemy's military affairs and reporting them to our army, if verified to be true, shall be rewarded according to their nature; 4. Causing significant military losses to the enemy, such as burning the enemy's food stations, camps, radio stations, power lines, military bridges, etc., if verified to be true, shall be rewarded according to their effects; 5. Other meritorious achievements similar to those listed above shall be rewarded accordingly. Article 8. If the meritorious achievements in the preceding article are particularly outstanding, in addition to being given a bonus, they may also be promoted to officers in the army according to their nature and qualifications. Article 9. Enemy officers and soldiers who can return with weapons or make meritorious contributions will be given a bonus and will still be recruited. Article 10. Ordinary people who have previously defected to the enemy, if they can realize their mistakes and return, will be exempted from punishment. Article 11. Matters not covered in these regulations may be amended by order at any time. Article 12. The area and date of implementation of these regulations will be announced separately by order.

Losses Suffered by the Japanese in the Invasion of the Four Northeastern Provinces: 140,000 Military and Civilian Casualties; Financial Losses of Several Million Yuan

Shenyang Dispatch: According to a recent statement released by a certain source, since 1931, the number of Japanese people killed and wounded in "Manchukuo" has been no less than 140,000. This loss is still continuing to grow. The Japanese have been constantly talking about the "restoration of Manchurian security," but the Japanese military authorities still insist on greatly increasing the number of troops in Manchuria, claiming that the territory is full of bandits. These two statements are vastly different. If one wants to know the truth, as always, one must seek it in the middle of the two extremes. According to the official figures reported by the Changchun Japanese police, banditry in 1935 was more serious than in 1934. The number of bandit appearances increased compared to before, the total number of bandits far exceeded the previous number, and the losses caused by the bandits greatly increased. No less than 21,000 people were kidnapped by bandits, more than 2,700 were killed, and more than 3,400 were wounded. There were a total of 5,800 arson cases, and the losses caused amounted to several trillion Japanese yen. According to several sources, the north has seen progress this year, but banditry in the east is still rampant. The most serious incident was when 2,000 bandits besieged Fushun, a major town in the northern section of Andong Province. According to official estimates on December 31, 1935, the total number of bandits was 33,605. As in previous years, the highest numbers were in August and September, usually above 65,000. Both of these numbers are significantly lower than those reported in the previous year, but the losses they caused have increased greatly. Now, it is still the season when bandits are most active. Although the monthly reports of each military district have been released, it is not yet possible to determine how the total number of bandits this year has increased or decreased compared to last year. Although there have been no reports of bandit attacks near the main railway lines and large towns, the seriousness of this major problem cannot be ignored. According to the Japanese authorities, the increase in Japanese immigrants can greatly help solve this difficulty. When Japanese people make up one-tenth of Manchuria's population in the future, the banditry problem will naturally be reduced to insignificance. The Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs are now both striving to make immigration to Manchuria a national policy of Japan. According to the Japanese military authorities, if northern Manchuria is heavily populated by Japanese, it will be possible to expand transportation, and transportation can be guaranteed during wartime. Several plans have now been proposed, one of which is to move 5 million Japanese to Manchuria in the next 20 years and 500,000 Koreans in the next 10 years. This plan is currently the most favored by the Japanese authorities. To promote Korean immigration to Manchuria, it is now proposed to establish a Korean Colonial Company with a capital of 10 million Japanese yen. Its headquarters will be located in Changchun. There will also be a Korean-Manchurian Colonial Company with a stipulated capital of 20 million Japanese yen. Its headquarters will be located in Seoul and will be established this month. Korean immigrants to Manchuria will strive to be located in the areas bordering Korea and in Jiandao Province. These immigrants are currently planned to be given 50 acres of land per person, with half of it cultivated, 45% used as pasture, and the remaining 5% used for building houses, warehouses, and vegetable gardens. Large-scale reclamation plans in the past have been abandoned because they were not suitable for large-scale immigration and would hire tenant farmers. Since these people have no land, they easily develop class divisions with those who own land. The Manchurian Colonial Company has already acquired 1.7 million acres of land near Jiamusi and is now planning to settle the first batch of immigrants there. This month, according to a statement from the Kwantung Army Headquarters, 500 Japanese soldiers will arrive in Manchuria in April next year to serve as the core of the new colony. The sixth group of immigrants is scheduled to depart at the beginning of this fiscal year, totaling 10,000 households, and will be scattered in the areas of Hulin, Gaoliuzhen (transliteration), and Aihui for reclamation. All three places are adjacent to the Soviet border. In addition, there are four other pieces of land, totaling 5 million acres, all adjacent to the Soviet border, which are planned for livestock farming. Furthermore, miners will also be settled in the Opura (transliteration) area near the Russian border, and 1.25 million acres of land will be demarcated in Jilin Province to settle forest workers. While the Japanese authorities are making every effort to move Japanese people to Manchuria, they are also making every effort to crack down on Chinese coolies entering Manchuria from Shandong Province, saying that their arrival in Manchuria will undermine the living standards of the Japanese. However, despite the crackdown, 10,472 people still landed in Dalian in July of this year, one-fifth of whom were entire families. In the same month, 7,542 people returned to the interior, only one-tenth of whom were entire families. It is estimated that the total number of coolies arriving in Manchuria in July of this year was more than 4,000 less than in the same month last year, and the net number was only 3,000. Compared with the number of people planned to be moved to Manchuria by the Japanese plan, the difference in quantity is incomparable.

The Yuehan Railway: The First Through Train Arrives in Wuchang

The entire trip took 45 hours and 30 minutes; the train traveled extremely smoothly and stopped at all 90 stations along the way; the railway administration's business policy is determined to become commercialized

Hankou Dispatch: The Yuehan Railway's first through train departed from Guangzhou South Station at 11:00 p.m. on the 1st, consisting of ten passenger cars, including one second-class car, two third-class cars, two third-class sleeper cars, one open car, one guard car, one dining car, one official car, and one baggage car. Because it was a passenger train, it did not carry cargo. Director Ling Hongxun stayed in Guangdong due to business, so Guangdong Operations Director Luo Nanke, Shaozhou Operations Director Fan Guanglian, Changsha Operations Director Huang Zhaodong, and others traveled north with the train. More than 160 passengers boarded the train in Guangdong. At 7:35 a.m. on the 2nd, the train passed Shaozhou. Because the section of the road from Shaozhou to Chenzhou was newly built, the train traveled slower. At 12:24 a.m., it passed Hengyang. At 7:49 a.m. on the 3rd, it passed Changsha. At 2:58 p.m., it passed Yuezhou. The train stopped briefly at all 90 stations along the way and traveled extremely smoothly. At 8:30 p.m., it arrived at the Xujiapeng Main Station in Wuchang. The entire trip took 45 hours and 30 minutes, only one and a half hours longer than the scheduled 44 hours, and two and a half hours shorter than the test run a few days ago, which took 48 hours. This result is truly gratifying. When the train arrived at Wuchang Station, although there were no grand ceremonies, no fewer than a thousand people gathered to watch, which shows that the public also knows the importance of this route. The train cars had white cloth banners with the words "Yuehan First Through Train." The approximately 300 passengers, upon disembarking, were all elated, because in addition to those who boarded in Guangzhou, no fewer than a hundred people boarded along the way. The first train departing from Xujiapeng, Wuchang, will depart south at 11:00 p.m. on the 4th and is expected to arrive in Guangzhou on the afternoon of the 6th. After that, two trains will run in both directions every five days. Daily service will only be possible after the new cars arrive. Fares are particularly low, with first-class tickets costing 36 yuan, second-class tickets costing 24 yuan, and third-class tickets costing 12 yuan. Cargo will be transported under a liability system, and fees will also be low. According to Deputy Director Zhou Zhongqi, the future business policy of this railway will be determined to become commercialized. Every employee must be close to merchants, and the business office will send personnel to various merchant firms and hotels to solicit cargo and provide sales assistance, so that the railway's cargo transportation will become increasingly developed. It is also planned to collect local specialties along the railway line at the end of this year and hold product exhibitions in Guangzhou and Hankou to attract the attention of merchants across the country. According to the railway's secretary, the entire railway was originally scheduled to be completed by the end of this year and open to traffic on New Year's Day next year. Through accelerated construction, it was able to open to traffic three months ahead of schedule. However, only a portion of the third-class cars ordered in England have arrived. The majority of the remaining cars will arrive by the end of the year. The cars currently in use are mostly borrowed from the Pinghan and Longhai Railways, so service is temporarily scheduled to run two trains in both directions every five days. Daily service can only be changed to daily service when there are sufficient cars. Furthermore, this trip took 45 and a half hours because of delays along the way. In the future, it can be reduced to 36 hours. If it is a special express train, it should be further shortened. To facilitate joint passenger and freight transport, the railway has decided to set up main stations and offices in Xujiapeng, Changsha, and Guangzhou. Whether the main office will be moved to Hengzhou is still undecided, because the center of the Yuehan Railway itself is Hengzhou, but the center of the Yuehan and Pinghan joint transport is Wuchang. (September 3rd)

Taicang: A Rape and Murder Case Occurs in Mao Market

Fan Daguan, a villager from the next map of Township 22 in Mao Market Township, District 6 of this county, lost his wife early and left behind a son who is fifteen years old this year. Now Lianbao has reached the age of consent, but Fan's son has not yet understood human affairs, so she has been having an affair with her neighbor Xu Afu across the river for a long time. Daguan entered the room to catch them in the act. Afu took out a knife to show his threat. Daguan disarmed him and stabbed him with the knife. With a cry, he died instantly. After someone reported it to Township Chief Gu Zheng, he telegraphed the responsible Fifth Substation, and the police arrested Fan Daguan and transferred him to the county. The corpse will be inspected by the county commissioner Shen Cheng and the examiner will go to the township to inspect it today.

Gu Fuqi, an employee of the parcel room of the Muyi Postal Administration, committed suicide by electric shock in the early morning of the 26th of last month. Bengbu Hongze Lake Bandits Rampant
