Local News

Liangguang Salt Transport Envoy Tang Haian Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon, Reportedly Summoned by Finance Minister Kong to Discuss Salt Administration, Liangguang Salt Tax Has Increased After Reorganization, Guishi Can Be Resolved Within One or Two Weeks

Mr. Tang Haian, Liangguang Salt Transport Envoy and Senior Advisor to the Finance Department of Guangdong Province, previously served as the Supervisor of the Jianghai Customs. Before the Cantonese Bureau was pacified, he went south on official business and then assumed his current position. He was summoned by Finance Minister Kong and arrived in Shanghai on the Blue Funnel Line's Cling Line (the Hong Kong telegram mistakenly reported as the Baodan Line) at about 12:00 noon yesterday. The ship docked at the company's wharf in Pudong. Mr. Tang changed to a small boat and landed at the New Customs Wharf, then returned to his private residence on Ferguson Road to rest. At 3:30 in the afternoon, Zhu Changnian, the current Supervisor of the Jianghai Customs, paid a visit and had a long conversation. Later, at about 6:00, Mr. Tang went to the Central Bank to meet with Finance Minister Kong for a long talk, discussing everything in detail. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency paid a special visit to his residence yesterday and was told the following:

Summoned by Kong to Discuss Salt Administration

Mr. Tang first said that he had previously submitted a detailed plan report on the reorganization of the Liangguang salt administration to Minister Kong by airmail. He then received a telegram from Minister Kong, ordering him to come north to discuss it in person, so he rushed to Shanghai. When he would return to the south would depend on when he had met Minister Kong to discuss various matters.

Reasons for the Past Depression of Salt Tax

Chen Jizhou, the Liangguang Salt Transport Envoy, served for eight years. Only in 1932 did the revenue reach 12 million. After that, it was only 9 million per year. The reason for the depression was entirely due to the negligence in suppressing smuggling. Chen reorganized all 25 tax police teams in various places into special service regiments, totaling 3,000 people, and transferred the 12 anti-smuggling fleets to the Provincial Anti-Smuggling Headquarters, entrusting the headquarters to handle salt smuggling on its behalf. For this reason, maritime and land smugglers of illicit salt did whatever they wanted.

Revenue Has Increased Greatly Since the Reorganization

The increase in salt tax depends on the strength of our anti-smuggling efforts. After I took office, in view of this, I first restored the tax police and reduced it to 18 teams, about 2,000 people, and assigned them to various places. I also recovered the 12 fleets from the Provincial Anti-Smuggling Headquarters, repaired them, and distributed them to six gates (namely Humen, etc.), and abolished the special tax plus two, special tax plus three, and leaky illegal tax items during Chen's tenure. Although I have been in office for less than a month, in this month, the tax revenue has increased by hundreds of thousands invisibly. If there are no military obstacles in the future, it can increase to 18 million per year.

Future Prospects for Salt Tax

Seven years ago, Guangxi used to buy Cantonese salt. Recently, it has changed to buying Vietnamese salt. If the Guizhou situation is settled, Cantonese salt will be promoted to Guangxi again, and the annual tax revenue will increase by several million more. Also, southern Jiangxi and southern Hunan also used to eat Cantonese salt seven years ago, but later changed to buying Huai salt. In the future, when the whole line of the Yuehan Railway is open to traffic, it will only take one day for Cantonese salt to be transported to Hunan and Jiangxi, which is convenient for transportation and the salt price is relatively low. Once promoted, the annual tax revenue can increase by several million more. It is estimated that the Liangguang salt tax revenue can reach 26 million to 28 million at the highest level each year.

Frugality of Expenses, Prudent Use of People

Regarding expenses, under Chen Weizhou's tenure, the annual cost was 1.8 million. I have been ordered by Minister Kong to make every effort to be frugal. The current budget only requires 180,000 per year, that is, within a month of my arrival, it has been reduced by more than 600,000. In one or two months, it can still be reduced by 100,000 to 200,000. At present, there are more than 1,000 internal and external staff (excluding tax police and fleets). Regarding the use of people, we must be prudent. They must be qualified, have reliable guarantees, and pay more attention to their personality and moral cultivation. We must ensure that tax officials are honest and incorruptible. For example, fleet officers must have nautical knowledge and be well-trained. Everything is based on the central tax police system. In the future, it is best to set up a special school for special training, but this is just a suggestion and must be decided by Minister Kong.

Guangdong Province's Finances Are Gradually on Track

Then the reporter asked about the financial situation of Guangdong Province. Mr. Tang said that the finances of Guangdong Province were chaotic in the past. He had been ordered to travel back and forth many times. Since the government problem was resolved, Director Song (Ziliang) has been working hard to reorganize the finances, abolishing the past deformed tax revenue agencies one by one. The lineup of each agency has been refreshed. Although it has not been long, it has gradually been on track. In the past, the monthly income was 6 million, but now it can reach 8 million. I still remember when Minister Song (Ziwen) was in Guangdong, it reached 14 million. With the efforts of Director Song, it will also reach 14 million in the future. As for the reform of the currency system, Minister Kong previously sent two Vice Ministers Zou (Lin) and Xu (Kan), Director Wu (Qiding), Vice President Chen (Xing), Tang Shoumin, Bei Songsun, and others to the south to hold dozens of meetings. Although various problems cannot be completely resolved overnight, they are generally resolved. After Minister Kong's review, the current price of Guangdong currency and legal currency is set at a ratio of 1.5 yuan to 1 yuan. In the future, miscellaneous currencies will be gradually withdrawn and the legal currency system will be completed. In the past, when Ou Fangpu was the director of the Department of Finance, there was only 100 million taels of silver, but the issuance of banknotes reached 250 million, a huge difference. Now the financial situation is stable, and the people of Guangdong Province are satisfied with the government's facilities.

Resolution of Guizhou Situation Is a Matter of One or Two Weeks

The reporter also asked about the Guizhou situation. Mr. Tang replied that regarding the situation in Guizhou Province, he was not a political person and did not know much. However, according to his observation, the resolution of the Guizhou situation was a matter of one or two weeks, and special peace was still in progress. At the end of the speech, Mr. Tang said that if a person is serious in doing things, he will inevitably be envied. At the beginning of his tenure, he received more than 3,000 letters of introduction from all parties seeking employment. Due to the limited scope of funds, he was unable to extend them all, causing disappointment. He only knew to obey the party and the country, and had no other plans.

Various Circles Smuggling Suppression Association Telegraphed to Stop Hebei-Chahar New Tax, Trade Union Federation Telegraphed Song Zheyuan to Ask for the Truth

The Shanghai Various Circles Smuggling Suppression Association yesterday telegraphed President Jiang of the Executive Yuan, "President Jiang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, since smuggled goods are dumped in various places, the loss of customs duties is not small, and the industrial and commercial enterprises run by Chinese people have suffered a great blow. Fortunately, our authorities have made a wise decision and promulgated the Anti-Smuggling Regulations. Industrial and commercial groups and people who care about the national economy in various places have also risen up to jointly report smuggled goods and support the national economy. The rampant situation has been slightly curbed. Recently, I read in the newspapers that the Hebei-Chahar Political Committee has decided to set up a new inspection office in Tianjin for smuggled goods from September 1, and will levy a new tax, which is about one-eighth of the current customs duty. Goods that have paid this tax are allowed to circulate in Hebei and Chahar. After learning about it, I was shocked. The Hebei-Chahar Political Committee's measures not only violate public opinion and destroy industry and commerce, but also shamelessly pander to foreigners and openly destroy the national regulations. Its drawbacks are that smuggled goods will rely on the one-eighth tax symbol to dump in the Hebei-Chahar market, which will devour the Chinese industries in the two provinces. Moreover, Japanese factories in North China are very developed in manufacturing. Now, with the low-cost raw materials, they can produce goods and dump them in South China. The impact will affect the economy of all provinces, and the collapse is still worrying. At this time, international commercial competition is becoming increasingly acute. All countries are relying on high tariffs to resist. Now, the Hebei-Chahar authorities are degrading tax rates and making a cocoon, which is extremely absurd. It is difficult to remain silent about the rise and fall of industry and commerce and the safety of the national economy. I respectfully request the Executive Yuan to strictly stop it, so as to maintain the national regulations and the people's livelihood. The Shanghai Various Circles Smuggling Suppression Association respectfully kowtows."

The Trade Union Federation yesterday telegraphed Chairman Song of the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee in Peiping, "Recently, there have been rumors that your association has decided to levy a new tax on goods transported into Tianjin from September 1, and will levy one-eighth of the current customs duty, that is, it will be allowed to circulate within the territory and will be protected by the authorities. This unfounded statement can be dismissed as nonsense, but since the smuggling problem in North China occurred, the national finances and the national industry and commerce have been affected. Fortunately, the central government has strictly stopped it, and it has only slightly reversed the decline. You are sitting in the north, and you must also be worried about this situation, planning the overall situation, seeking a whole solution, and fulfilling the expectations of the people. You know that what is said on the way is exaggerated, but for the sake of stabilizing all industries, I have to telegraph your association to indicate the truth in order to dispel doubts. Furthermore, if the previous news is true, a large number of smuggled goods will be imported from North China again, gradually advancing south and spreading to various places. Not only will our country's tariff barriers be completely destroyed, but also the industrial and commercial industries will inevitably collapse, and the impact on the people's livelihood will be even greater than before. What I think is dangerous, I cannot remain silent, so I dare to attach it. I hope you will consider it carefully. The Chinese Industrial General Federation respectfully kowtows."

All Students Must Use X-ray Examination, Municipal Education Bureau Notifies All Schools to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday instructed all schools in the city, "According to the report of Gu Yuqi, the president of the private Tongde Medical College, the rise and fall of a country depends on the strength of the nation, and the strength of the nation must depend on the health of the people's physical fitness. Therefore, health is an important plan for the revival of the nation today, and an urgent task that cannot be delayed for saving the country and survival. Today's students are at the time of youth growth, and they are also the key to the strength of our future nation. Those who are teachers and guardians should cherish and protect them, so that they have a healthy physique and become useful talents for the country and the nation. It is necessary to prepare for the future and catch up in a hurry. The harvest of the mulberry tree is still not too late. The college previously received an order from the ministry that all new students at the time of enrollment, and old students at the beginning of each academic year, must conduct a detailed physical examination once, which shows that the central authorities have also paid attention to it. Its importance does not need to be stated again. However, with ordinary physical examinations, it is difficult to accurately diagnose whether students' physical fitness is truly healthy and whether diseases are hidden internally. In a school with a large number of students, living together all day long, the spread of diseases is always worrying. The college has seen this, and has decided to add X-ray examinations to the new and old students from this semester, in addition to physical examinations, in order to see the key to the problem and show caution. However, this examination is related to the health of school groups, and is not limited to one school. It is requested that the bureau appreciate the importance of this prevention work, and allow all new and old students of the schools in the city to undergo this X-ray examination at the time of enrollment. In order to achieve popularization, the college will only charge a handling fee of one yuan per person for professors and new and old students from all schools to come to the Tongde Hospital affiliated to the college (address: No. 1, Lane 67, Tongfu Road, New Quanpu Road), and elementary school students can also be reduced appropriately, or it can be approved and complied with by the bureau. As for the time, it is scheduled from 10:00 to 12:00 every morning. If there are too many people, you can negotiate in advance and agree on a time to prepare. Is it appropriate? I respectfully ask for verification and immediate implementation, so as to emphasize public health and benefit the prevention of tuberculosis. According to this, the prevention of tuberculosis is indeed important. Now the preferential treatment measures have been discussed and decided. A handling fee of one yuan will be charged for X-ray examination of the lungs for students of specialized subjects and above, eight corners for middle school students, and six corners for elementary school students. All should be examined from September 1 to the end of October this year. The order is hereby issued for all schools to comply with."

The Municipal National Election Promotion Association Yesterday Issued an Announcement to All Citizens, Registration Without Oath Has No Civil Rights, I Hope All Citizens of the City Will Enthusiastically Participate in the Oath

Since the establishment of the Municipal National Election Promotion Association, all parties have paid a lot of attention to it. The association yesterday issued an announcement to the public, the original text is recorded as follows, "Dear citizens of the city, the National Assembly will be opened in Nanjing on November 12 this year. All people of the Republic of China who are 20 years old, regardless of gender, rich or poor, or whether they have been educated, as long as they have not committed a crime, as long as they do not have mental illness, have gone through civil registration and civil oath, and have obtained civil rights, can have the right to elect National Assembly representatives or be elected as National Assembly representatives. Everyone knows that the National Assembly is an important hub for our country to transition from the period of political tutelage to the period of constitutional government. The success or failure of the National Assembly can determine the future of our country. Therefore, all of us who are loyal to the Republic of China, for the sake of the future of the country, must not only not give up the right to elect representatives to the assembly, but also properly use this right to elect appropriate representatives to the assembly according to ideal standards. If the members of the assembly are good, the results of the assembly will naturally be good. Therefore, we must not relax our efforts to obtain civil rights and the right to vote. We must go through civil registration, and we must hold civil oaths. Otherwise, all the rights that citizens should enjoy cannot be fully enjoyed and exercised. Needless to say, he has no part in the election or election of National Assembly representatives. Now, civil registration in our Shanghai has been completed, and civil oaths will soon be held in various districts. The association hereby hopes that all citizens of Shanghai, if they have already gone through civil registration, must go to take the civil oath on time after the date of the oath is announced. This is our right and our obligation. Whoever gives up civil registration and civil oath gives up civil qualification, and is outside the Republic of China. It should also be noted that the first necessary condition for obtaining civil rights is to go through registration, and the second necessary condition after registration is to take the oath. If you only register but do not participate in the oath ceremony, then the citizen's certificate cannot be obtained, and civil rights cannot be exercised. Therefore, registration alone is not enough. It is necessary to participate in the oath to be considered to have met the statutory procedures and to have obtained the statutory qualifications. Now the oath will be held soon, please pay attention to the date."

Chambers of Commerce, Journalists, and Education, Three Units Tomorrow to Elect Candidates, Education Groups Swore Oath Yesterday

Yesterday, citizen oath registration was held for groups, members of the Education Association, university and college faculty, and the Jiangnan Shipyard. Employees from the two railway bureaus, Shanghai Cement Company, and other organizations also participated. Tomorrow (the 6th), the Chambers of Commerce, Journalists Association, and education groups, three units, will hold elections. Each of these groups should put forth candidates for the National Assembly representatives. Details are as follows:

Yesterday's Oath-Taking Situation

Members of the eleven district education associations affiliated with the Municipal Education Association, as well as faculty and staff from public and private universities and independent colleges, who had not taken the oath previously, took the oath in nine locations including the Municipal Education Association yesterday. From morning till night, participation was extremely high. The National Election Office dispatched Lin Meiyan and Huang Tiren to oversee the oaths. At the Shanghai Cement Company, Beipiao Wharf, Wing On Textile Factory, Jiangnan Shipyard, and the two railway bureau administrations, employee oaths were held separately yesterday morning. The office dispatched Ding Shoutang, Shi Renzheng, Wang Chenge, Yang Dean, and Tan Peiyan to oversee the oaths. The Songhu Garrison Headquarters also held citizen registration oaths for officers at the headquarters yesterday morning, presided over by Commander Yang, with Jiang Huaisu overseeing. In total, approximately 20,000 people took the oath in various locations yesterday.

Three Groups to Elect Tomorrow

The office has already notified and instructed the executive personnel of the Chambers of Commerce, Journalists Association, and Education Association to hold separate elections for candidates representing their respective units tomorrow at three locations: the Municipal Chambers of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge, the Journalists Association at the Dalu Commercial Building, and the Municipal Education Association at Daji Road. The times are as follows: Chambers of Commerce from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, Journalists Association from 3:00 PM to 4:00 PM, and Education Association from 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM.

Method for Electing Representatives

According to the election law, the election of representatives from professional groups or freelance professional groups, if the group has multiple levels, should be conducted by the executive organs and staff of its lowest-level group. Therefore, tomorrow for the three groups, except for the Journalists Association, which has no lower-level organization and should have all its executive committee members present to elect, the Chambers of Commerce should have the executive committee members of each trade association established before the promulgation of the election law and already affiliated with the Municipal Chambers of Commerce present to elect. The education groups should have the directors of each district education association and the presidents, deans, and secretaries-general of national or registered private universities and independent colleges present to elect. All personnel with the right to elect must have already registered as citizens. Therefore, they must bring their own group or school certificate and citizen certificate when attending to receive election ballots and have the right to elect. Furthermore, the qualifications of candidates are as follows according to law: (1) Have the qualifications of an elector, (2) be at least 25 years old, (3) have been engaged in the profession for more than three years (intermittent periods can be combined), (4) currently be a member of the group. Electors should pay attention to these points. As for the number of candidates to be elected, it should be the same as the number of representatives that each group should send (i.e., four for the Chambers of Commerce, eleven for the Journalists Association, and eighteen for Education). After the ballots are counted, three times the number of representatives will be selected and submitted to the National Government for designation.

Chambers of Commerce Notice to Associations

The Shanghai Municipal Chambers of Commerce issued an urgent notice yesterday, stating, "Regarding the notice, on the 4th of this month, we received Instruction No. 28 from the Shanghai Municipal Representative Election Office of the National Assembly, stating that the period for the Chambers of Commerce groups to elect candidates is scheduled for 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM on September 6th at the Chambers of Commerce headquarters. In addition to publishing the notice in the newspaper, we are enclosing the "Instructions for Electing Candidates." We order your association to instruct the executive committee members of each affiliated trade association to bring their respective association certificates and their own citizen certificates and to go on time to elect according to law. Attached are five copies of the "Instructions for Electing Candidates" and send our greetings. The attached instructions for electing candidates are as follows: (1) Only the executive committee members of each group are eligible to vote (for the Lawyers Association, only the standing committee members are eligible). They must be present in person and cannot delegate representatives. (2) Voters must present their group certificates and their own citizen certificates to receive election ballots. (3) If voters cannot write their ballots themselves, they may request the voting supervisor to designate someone to write the ballot for them, but they must sign or stamp it themselves, or affix a fingerprint. (4) After voters have finished writing their ballots, they should immediately put them into the ballot box themselves. (5) If voters meet any of the conditions in Article 61 of the Implementing Regulations of the Election Law, the voting supervisor may order them to leave the polling place.

Zhejiang Consolidates Class A Public Bonds, Exchange and Redemption Today, Face Value of 4.5 Million, First Principal Repayment in November

The Zhejiang Provincial Government's newly issued consolidation public bonds, totaling 60 million yuan, have been printed by the Commercial Press. The Department of Finance has scheduled to entrust the Central, China, Communications, and Zhejiang Local Banks in Hangzhou to begin exchanging and redeeming Class A bond certificates from the 5th. It will also reorganize the fund management committee to establish creditworthiness. The details are as follows:

Exchange for New Certificates

The bond certificates to be exchanged from the 5th are the Class A (i.e., first category) bond certificates of the consolidation public bonds. The face value is 4.5 million yuan, totaling 58,600 certificates. After these bond certificates were transported from Shanghai to Hangzhou, the Department of Finance added seals and signatures and distributed them to the Central, China, Communications, and Local Banks for safekeeping. The exchange will begin simultaneously on the 5th at the banks' branches and offices in various locations. Holders of the three types of bonds issued by Zhejiang Province in April 17th, the public bonds for repaying old debts, the highway public bonds issued in July of the same year, and the periodic loan certificates issued in the 23rd year, except for those that have already been drawn and will not be exchanged, can obtain application forms from the commissioned banks' branches in various locations and apply to exchange for new bonds according to the prescribed procedures.

Fund Establishment

In order to establish creditworthiness, the Zhejiang Department of Finance plans to reorganize the Provincial Bond Fund Management Committee this month. Representatives from the Ministry of Finance, the Auditing Department, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, the Zhejiang Provincial Federation of Commerce, the Municipal Chambers of Commerce, the Bankers Association, the Money Dealers Association, and bondholders will be jointly organized. The date for the first lottery repayment of the consolidated new public bonds is scheduled to be held on November 11th of this year.

Inspection of Artificial Silk Fabrics Transport and Sales, Temporary Approval of Association Certification, Exchange Licenses with Certificates, Effective Today

In order to prevent smuggling, the Ministry of Finance promulgated the "Inspection and Clearance Methods for Artificial Silk Woven Native Goods Pitoo," stipulating that a "License for Transporting and Selling Artificial Silk" must be presented to exchange for a "License for Transporting and Selling Pitoo." Because very few silk factories in China directly import materials and produce and sell their own products, most silk factories are transferred by silk shops to Shanghai and distributed to various locations. If the previous regulations are followed, it will be impossible to transport and sell. Therefore, the Shanghai Silk Industry Association and the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Weaving Federation repeatedly petitioned the Ministry of Finance and other agencies to change the regulations. Yesterday, Wu Xingcha and Lou Fengshao again petitioned the Jianghai Customs and the General Tax Office. They reached an agreement after discussion. Before the Ministry of Finance's relief measures are announced, the industry association will temporarily be allowed to issue certificates to exchange for transport and sales licenses to facilitate transportation. This measure will be implemented starting today.

Wuhu has long been operating, but because of the spring famine, operations were suspended. There are also many factories, shops, and transportation companies that have resumed business or newly opened after autumn that have not registered. If registration is not supplemented to facilitate transportation and sales, or even if their operations are temporarily suspended, commerce and the people's livelihood will be affected. Special Transportation Prices for Cotton Yarn, Approved by Ministry for One-Year Extension

Special prices for cotton yarn and cotton woven goods transported between Beijing and Shanghai were established last year, namely, full carloads are not reduced from the original grade. Those reported by the China Cotton Mill Federation with credentials are reduced by 20 percent. Less than full carloads are reduced by 20 percent from the original grade. Those reported by the Federation with credentials are further reduced by 20 percent. This regulation expired on August 31 of this year. The bureau submitted a report to the Ministry of Railways, which approved it on September 1. The extension will continue for one year from September 1.

Opium Addicts in This City Actively Register, More Than 200 Go to the Bureau to Register Daily, Opium Addiction Hospitals Are Overcrowded

Since the Municipal Public Security Bureau was ordered to handle opium prohibition matters, it has been actively progressing with considerable results. The reporting and registration of opium addicts has reached more than 50,000. The original deadline for registration was the end of last month. However, in order to give opium addicts a final opportunity to reform, a special request was made to the opium prohibition supervisor to extend the deadline by ten days, deciding that it would end on the 10th of this month. There are still five days left. Yesterday, a reporter from the National News Agency went to the Public Security Bureau to interview Section Chief Dai of the Opium Addict Registration Section in order to understand the latest situation of opium prohibition. According to the interview, the section is responsible for handling opium prohibition matters in the city. Recently, during the extension period, opium addicts have realized that it is wrong to delay and evade registration. More than 200 people a day have voluntarily gone to the bureau to register and confess. Approximately 20 to 30 people a day have voluntarily requested to be sent to a hospital to quit opium. As a result, the Municipal Shanghai North and Shanghai South Opium Addiction Hospitals, the Opium Addiction Prison, and the Longhua Detoxification Center are filled with opium addicts. There are no vacant beds. Those currently requesting to quit opium must register in advance and wait their turn to enter the hospital. This shows the enthusiasm of opium addicts to confess. However, the section still sends staff out every day to supervise the various branches and teams to diligently investigate in order to achieve the goal of registering all opium addicts in the city and prohibiting them step by step. If opium addicts fail to report before the deadline, they will be sent to the Garrison Headquarters for severe punishment according to law, with no leniency.

Central Civil Training Department Explains Organization of Private Associations

According to Dagong news agency, the Central Public Training Department issued an order yesterday to the party departments of various provinces and cities to explain the handling of existing private associations. The original order stated, "The Zhejiang Provincial Executive Committee submitted a report stating that the District Executive Committee of Yunhe County reported that there were private association organizations among the people in the county. The number of people ranges from three to dozens, with a long history. They also bought租石 (rent stones) and held a聚餐 (feast) once a year. The purpose is聚餐 (feasting), or studying literature, or connecting feelings, or worshiping a certain god. Therefore, the names are a certain association, a certain club. It is necessary to investigate and register this type of organization. However, since there are non-religious cultural charity groups, what procedures should be used to register has not been clearly stipulated. The facts are listed in detail and a request for explanation is made as follows: (1) This type of association organization belongs to文人 (literati) and worships Zhu Wengong and Wenchang Dijun. It belongs to the general public, then it is called the Bai Xiang Hui (Worship Incense Association) and still worships gods, such as the Land Association and the Lady Association. The purpose is pure and there is no illegal action. It should fulfill the registration. How should it be registered? Please explain this. (2) Associations that have not been registered by party and government agencies are not legal organizations. What method should be used to suppress or force the registration of the above associations? Please explain this. (3) The annual consumption of the association is quite large. Can we persuade them to organize rural cooperative societies with the money that should be consumed, or use political power to correct the association's property and allocate production facts? Please indicate this. Regarding the above three points, we hereby submit a document requesting your association to explain and follow it. It is convenient for the party and so on. Based on this, the various situations mentioned are not unique to that county. The headquarters has not been able to decide how to deal with it. In addition to replying, we hereby submit a document requesting your review and explanation. Regarding the three points for which an explanation is requested, the headquarters has replied as follows: (1) Associations that have the nature of academic research or improving customs should be listed as cultural groups. Associations with public welfare nature should be listed as public welfare groups. Associations that belong to the above two types should guide the community to apply for filing according to law. (2) In addition to promoting superstition and harming social安宁 (peace and tranquility), the guidance of existing civil associations should be notified to government agencies at any time to suppress them. The method of persuasion should be used. (3) Associations that belong to the category of economic mutual assistance may, depending on the nature, guide them to establish various cooperative societies in a persuasive manner. In addition to replying by letter, please check and forward it to be observed and handled carefully."

Labor Strike at Five Silk Weaving Factories in West Shanghai, Mediation Successful at Three Factories, Two Factories Resume Strike, Officials Schedule Mediation on the 7th

The workers at the five silk weaving factories in the West Shanghai area, including Baohua, Yucun, Yiyou, Tiancheng, and Yongfeng, went on strike to demand increased wages. After party and government agencies sent personnel to persuade them to resume work first, the Social Affairs Bureau specially convened both labor and management the day before yesterday to mediate according to law. The two parties agreed and signed a settlement record for the Yiyou, Tiancheng, and Yongfeng factories. However, the mediation at the Baohua and Yucun factories failed. Starting yesterday, the workers at these two factories went on strike again. It has now been scheduled for the 7th to mediate again. The settlement methods for the Yiyou and other three factories are recorded as follows: (1) Yiyou, the wages for plain satin are uniformly calculated at four and three-tenths cents per meter. The artificial silk crepe is uniformly increased by 8 percent from the original wage. The wages for the preparation department are uniformly increased by 5 percent. (2) Tiancheng, the wages for four-inch single crepe in the weaving department are increased by five cents from the original. The wages for the preparation department are uniformly increased by 5 percent. (3) Yongfeng, plain satin is increased by five cents per foot from the original wage. True silk satin is increased by six cents per meter from the original wage. The wages for the preparation department are restored from 90 percent to 95 percent.

Nagasaki Maru Collided with Mingsheng Ship in the Huangpu River Yesterday, Gonghe Ship Collided as Well

The Mingsheng, a steamer of Ewo Yanghsing Company, was on a regular voyage to the South Seas. It had sailed from Guangzhou, Hong Kong and Swatow to Shanghai this time. It entered the port at 12:20 PM yesterday and was about to sail to Shun Tai Wharf for berthing. Before arriving at the wharf, it stopped and turned around. It was docking when the Nagasaki Maru of Japan Mail Steamship Co. also entered the port. The Nagasaki Maru was about to reach the Hongkou River surface. At that time, the Mingsheng had turned around and was berthing. The Nagasaki Maru was also sailing to that area and was preparing to turn around and prepare to berth at Huishan Wharf. However, it was high tide and the water was very rough. The Nagasaki Maru was trying to turn its body, and its bow slammed into the

Mingsheng Ship

Because the Mingsheng had stopped to berth, it was inevitable. With a bang, the bow of the Mingsheng was hit by the Nagasaki Maru. Because the force was too great, the body of the Mingsheng was pushed back after being hit. The Gonghe, an Ewo Yangtze River ship, which was berthed behind the Mingsheng, was also hit by the stern of the Mingsheng, which hit the bow of the Gonghe. The Gonghe also shook. As a result, the Mingsheng

Bow and Stern Were Damaged

Because the stern rudder blade happened to hit the bow of the Gonghe, it was badly damaged, and the bow was severely injured by the Nagasaki Maru. The Nagasaki Maru and the Gonghe received very little damage. After the accident, both parties sent personnel to survey the damage. At the same time, they reported to the company and the Customs Port Authority for inspection. The Mingsheng could only quickly unload passengers and cargo from the ship to the wharf. The ship was originally scheduled to sail to Qingdao today to transport goods. Because the ship was damaged and could not sail without repairs, it was decided yesterday afternoon to temporarily cancel the voyage to Qingdao and prepare to enter the factory for major repairs.

New Suspects Apprehended in Japanese Sailor Case: Closed-Door Trial, Details Unknown, Detention Extended for Further Questioning

The case of the murdered Japanese sailor, Hideo Nakayama, has been under investigation due to the complexity of evidence and the time required for the investigation. Recently, the Public Concession Police apprehended two more suspects: Zhu Guisheng from Yangzhou and Jin Daoquan from Jiangbei. They are suspected of involvement in the Nakayama case and the murder of Japanese man Kanzo Kayao. Both men were handed over to the First Special District Court for detention, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The police have also discovered that Zhang Yuhua (also known as Zhang Shimin, also known as Zhang Wei, 36 years old) from Baoying, who was arrested by inland authorities for the assassination attempt on President Wang Jingwei, is significantly related to both the Nakayama and Kayao cases. A request has been made to the Jiangsu High Court to transfer him. The request was approved, and he has been transferred from the capital to Shanghai and detained at the Songhu Garrison Command. He was brought back to the police station by Western Detective Krote the day before yesterday. Because Zhang was ill, he was sent to the Municipal Council Hospital for treatment. Simultaneously, Chen Siming (32 years old) from Yangzhou, who is believed to be involved in both cases, was also apprehended. Yesterday morning, the police escorted Chen and Zhang to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu, based on Articles 76 and 101 of the Criminal Procedure Law, requested detention for further investigation. Due to the seriousness of the case, he also requested a closed-door trial, which was approved by Judge Zhong Qing. Therefore, the details of the trial are unknown. The judge then immediately announced the approval of detention and adjourned the hearing for further review. The number of Chinese arrested in connection with the Nakayama case has reached seven: Yang Wendao, Ye Haisheng, Zhou Sherong, Zhu Guisheng, Jin Daoquan, Chen Siming, and Zhang Yuhua.

Development Plan for Ziti Town in Western Shanghai: Welcoming Investment to Revitalize Industry

Ziti Town (i.e., Zhuzhai) is located at the border of this city and Jiading and Qingpu counties, less than twenty li from this city. In the past, traffic was blocked, forming a closed-off situation. Since the autumn of the year before last, thanks to donations from local gentry such as Hou Shuda, the Puzhanzhai Road was built and connected to Caoyadu and other roads in western Shanghai, greatly improving traffic. Recently, Hou Shuda, Huang Chengbo, Zhu Jingyu, Zhu Qin Yuan, and others have proposed dredging the Panlong River to connect it with the Suzhou Creek (Wusong River). If the dredging is successful, ships of several hundred tons can pass through without obstacles. From then on, water and land transportation will be convenient, and the area will become an important town in western Shanghai. If businesses from all sectors come to build factories and farms to revitalize industry, they are sure to reap substantial profits. The price of land in the town is low (less than 500 yuan per mu). Those interested in investing can contact the four gentlemen: Hou, Huang, Zhu, and Zhu.

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a response to the Ministry of Industries yesterday regarding the decision to stop participating in the Texas Centennial Exposition in the United States, stating: "Submitted for reporting. Allegations of Preferential Purchases of Foreign Electrical Appliances Denied by Auditing Department, etc.: Reply to National Goods Federation

The Shanghai National Goods Promotion Federation received a letter from the Electrical Appliance Industry Association stating, "According to rumors from colleagues in the capital, the Auditing Department has designated a certain brand of foreign light bulbs, and the Railway Police Headquarters has designated a certain brand of foreign electric fans. Please send separate letters to the above two agencies to inquire about the truth." After the federation sent separate letters, it recently received replies from the Auditing Department and the Railway Police Headquarters stating that the light bulbs and electric fans they used were domestic Huade brand light bulbs and Huasheng brand electric fans. The allegations of designating the purchase of foreign electrical appliances are not true. The original letters stated: (1) Auditing Department's reply: "In reply to your letter, advocating national goods is the patriotic duty of our people. Your understanding of the greater good is admirable. The electrical appliances purchased for the construction of the new building by this department are indeed domestic Huade brand products, according to the contracting company. This department has not designated the use of foreign goods. The rumors are false and unfounded. We hereby reply to your inquiry. To the Shanghai National Goods Promotion Federation." (2) Railway Police Headquarters' reply: "In reply to your letter, we received your letter stating that according to rumors from colleagues in the capital, the Railway Police Headquarters has designated the use of a certain brand of foreign electric fans. Please inform us of the actual situation to dispel doubts. The electric fans and ceiling fans purchased by this bureau this year are produced by the domestic Huasheng Company. Ordinary purchases are also prioritized for domestic goods to promote them. The allegation of designating a certain brand of foreign electric fans is not true and is likely a misunderstanding. We hereby reply to your inquiry and hope you will check and correct the record. To the Shanghai National Goods Promotion Federation."

Fellow Villagers from Zhongshan County Discuss Repatriating Ancestral Remains for Burial

Zhongshan County is the hometown of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. It is estimated that no fewer than 40,000 to 50,000 villagers from Zhongshan are engaged in business or serving in Shanghai. Among them are leaders and talents in the political and business circles, such as Wu Tiecheng, Yu Hongjun, Chen Bingqian, Cai Zengji, Guo Shun, Zheng Bozhao, Wang Yunwu, and Yang Meinan, all well-known figures in society. Recently, due to the low-lying and damp terrain of the GuangZhao Old Cemetery in Chedaijiao and its proximity to the Suzhou River, which has been plagued by floods in recent years, the remains of deceased villagers from Zhongshan buried there have not been properly settled. A movement has been launched to collectively relocate the remains of deceased villagers to Xinzhuang for burial to comfort the wandering souls and properly honor the ancestors. A general meeting of the initiators will be held at 2:00 PM on the 6th of this month at the Yueqiao Commercial Federation on Bazhi Road to discuss everything and jointly plan the undertaking. Zhongshan County has always been known as a model county, and it is certain that it will fully demonstrate its spirit of unity in carrying out this public welfare undertaking that concerns the county. It is reported that the current committee members preparing for the meeting are Chen Bingqian, Li Yunshan, Shen Linsheng, Li Huasheng, Gao Jieyuan, Yang Fengyao, Li Fengzhang, Chen Shounan, Yang Huiji, Zheng Xiufen, Wei Zhiting, Zhong Zhinan, Zheng Yaotang, and others.

Page 16

Abolishing Extra Tips: Hotel Workers' Union Pours Out Its Views; Stipulate Wage Amounts with Reference to Hangzhou and Nanjing Examples; Eliminate the Evil Habit of Hotels Collecting Security Deposits

The Shanghai Hotel Industry Workers' Union, for the New Life Movement Promotion Association, improves bad habits and abolishes extra tips. The union has been collecting opinions from members across the city for days and submitted them to the Shanghai New Life Cadre Association. The original text is as follows: "Submitted to plead for sympathy for the hardships of workers, determine salaries, protect security deposits, split tips, to implement the New Life Movement, thoroughly eradicate bad habits, cultivate good habits, and maintain the new movement. This union received a notice from your association to attend the New Life Discussion Meeting. At the first meeting, we read the New Life General Association's principles and implementation methods for abolishing extra tips. We understand that the implementation of the New Life Movement is something that the public should sincerely follow. The government and civil servants should also supervise its practice. Therefore, the abolition of extra tips is undoubtedly necessary. This union, in view of the fact that the abolition of this extra tip relates to the survival of all members of the union, specially convened a meeting of members on August 1 to discuss it. We resolved and reported the methods to your association, and submitted them to the meeting for discussion on file. After three meetings, we passed the draft implementation methods and requested the cadre association to pass and implement them. This union has to state the actual situation. We sincerely request your association to consider the suffering of workers so that workers under heavy restrictions of bad habits can be free from unreasonable restraint. The original intention of the New Life Movement to improve bad habits can also be implemented. Shanghai is the hub of national industry and commerce, a place of international attention. In recent years, the market has been depressed, factories have closed, and stores have closed. The decline of industry and commerce is indeed a fact. However, although the employees of various industries have also suffered considerable losses from the suspension or bankruptcy of their businesses, the impact on waiters is particularly great and profound when hotels go bankrupt or suspend operations. Bankruptcies have been seen and heard from time to time in recent years, but new hotels continue to open, an abnormal situation caused by using waiters' security deposits as capital. There is no guarantee in advance. Once a hotel suspends operations, it is not easy to return the security deposit. Most waiters are poor people from bankrupt rural areas seeking a living in the city. Eighty or ninety percent of the money for this security deposit comes from high-interest loans. Once the security deposit cannot be returned, they lack the funds to sue and lack the preparation to wait for a long time to earn a living. The various hardships are not known to outsiders. Moreover, waiters work long and hard hours, and their food and treatment are meager and harsh. They do not receive any salary, and they do not share in the tips. If they do not collect extra tips to make a living, how can the waiter's family survive? Therefore, this evil habit of collecting extra tips is actually cultivated by the greed of employers, not the waiter's original intention. In the process of national revival and the implementation of the New Life Movement, this unreasonable bad habit should be abolished to show determination. However, how to consider the lives of waiters after the abolition should also be decided first to facilitate implementation. Also, the huge security deposits collected by employers without any guarantee, which are used to supplement the employer's capital, is also one of the bad habits. It seems appropriate to plan for a safe way to ensure that social life and social order are both adjusted. After consideration by this union, we propose that your association refer to the examples of Nanjing and Hangzhou and separately stipulate the minimum and maximum wage amounts that waiters in large and small hotels should receive, the date and frequency of daily payment, and the method of splitting tips, and issue orders for uniform implementation throughout the city to alleviate the lives of waiters after the prohibition of extra tips. Furthermore, when hotels close down or go bankrupt, the right to priority compensation should be stipulated in the legislation for wages owed, which is only fair. As for guaranteeing security deposits, we propose that your association send a letter to the Bureau of Social Affairs to register all large and small hotels in the city, pay attention to their partners and capital amounts, and order them to provide a guarantee method for collecting waiters' security deposits. Those who violate the rules will be banned. In this way, the implementation of the New Life Movement will be smooth and unimpeded. Therefore, we have stated the reasons and submitted this document, requesting your association to review and approve it for the public convenience."

Murdered Female Corpse in Gunny Sack Examined by Court; Packet of White Powder Found in Stocking; Sent to Forensic Pathologist for Testing Before Further Review

At 5:42 AM the day before yesterday, Chinese Constable No. 1465 of the Hongkou Police Station was patrolling on McTaggart Road when he was informed that there was a discarded gunny sack in front of No. 192 on the road. Upon inspection, the constable found a female corpse, approximately 50 years old, with 17 knife wounds. After being informed, the police station dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. The body was then transported to the forensic examination office on Fieland Road to await examination. All details have been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Tang, appointed by the First Special District Court, along with forensic pathologist Zhang Yan and a clerk, arrived at the office to examine the body. Forensic pathologist Zhang and a doctor from the Municipal Council determined that the body had died 24 hours before it was discovered. After the detectives reported the investigation process, they stated that the body was hidden inside two gunny sacks sewn together. Three silver hairpins were found on the deceased's hair, and a small mirror with duck eggs on the side of her body, and a packet of white powder inside her left stocking. When questioned, the congee shop opposite No. 192 stated that they had not seen the gunny sack at 3:00 AM that morning. According to Lv Wenfu, who set up a bean curd stall at No. 194 McTaggart Road, at around 3:00 AM yesterday morning, he saw two or three passersby kicking and looking at the gunny sack, so he reported it to the Chinese constables. Based on Tang's testimony, the unidentified female corpse was confirmed to have been stabbed to death with a knife. Before the relatives are identified, the corpse will be handed over to the Pushan Junta for collection. The police station responsible for the case should strictly investigate and arrest the murderers. The white powder brought to the court by the Chinese detective will be handed over to the forensic pathologist for testing. As for the packet of white powder, it was hidden in a toothpaste powder bag, so it remains to be seen whether it is a drug or toothpaste powder. It needs to be clarified after the forensic pathologist's examination.

Zhang Pinfu (also known as Wu Pinfu, Xiao Wuxi, 24 years old), a native of Wuxi, lives at No. 14 Deyuan Lane, Yangshupu, and works as a coppersmith in the machinery room of the Shanghai Electric Power Company on the same road. Later, he learned that Afeng and Wang had an ambiguous relationship, leading to deep resentment. Recently, company workers often ridiculed Zhang, saying that Wang had leaked the secret.

Zhang was extremely humiliated. At 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, he saw Wang enter the toilet to defecate. Zhang obtained a triangular sharp blade from the machinery room and followed him in. Without saying a word, he pulled out the blade and stabbed Wang's head and abdomen, inflicting five wounds to the head and two to the abdomen. Wang collapsed to the ground in agony, crying for help. Zhang, knowing that he had committed a great crime, stabbed his own left leg to lessen his guilt and ran into the office, reporting to the Western staff member, Kleinmann, that Wang Jiasheng had stabbed him in the leg. Later, it was discovered that Wang had been stabbed in the toilet,

seriously injured,

and on the verge of death. Wang and Zhang were taken to Renji Hospital for treatment. Zhang seized the opportunity to escape and telegraphed the Yangshupu police station. Detective Chief Liu Wenzao, detective Su Yinggen, and detectives Zhang Guanying and Liu Changgen investigated and learned that Zhang Pinfu was hiding at his sister's place at No. 14 Xi Junan Lane, Tianbao Road, Zhabei. They rushed there and arrested him with the help of the Public Security Bureau's detectives. He was taken back to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, the police department's lawyer, Zhang Shizhu,

explained the case

to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. He filed a public prosecution under Article 171, Section 2, of the Criminal Code for murder. He also stated that the victim, Wang Jiasheng, was seriously injured in the hospital and might die. He requested a postponement and presented the doctor's injury report. Detective Liu reported the process of arresting the defendant and handed over the murder weapon and Wang Jiasheng's blood-stained felt hat and clothes as evidence. The Western staff member, Kleinmann, and the workers in the same truck, Chen Genfu, testified that two months ago, they heard others say that Wang and Zhang's wife had

a physical relationship, and Zhang wanted to kill Wang. Judge Zhong Qing questioned the defendant, who stated that Wang Jiasheng initially acted as a matchmaker, then tricked the woman into a hotel for sexual intercourse and he saw it. The next morning, they walked out together. After marriage, he repeatedly induced the wife to go out for secret dates, and in the company, he said that his wife was promiscuous and indecent. That is why he committed this crime. The rest of the confession was evasive. Wang's wife, Liu, stated that her husband acted as a matchmaker and did not have any improper advances towards Afeng. The defendant's accusation was false and requested judgment. Judge Zhong Qing ordered Zhang Pinfu to be returned to custody for further verification at a later date.

China International Famine Relief Commission Discusses Repairing Suiyuan Minsheng Canal

The Minsheng Canal is located in central Suiyuan Province, spanning the two counties of Salaqi and Tuoketuo. The canal entrance is located 30 li east of Baotou Town. Its irrigation area is bounded by the Yellow River to the southwest, the Ping Sui Railway to the north, and the Dahei River to the east, and can irrigate 1.2 million mu of farmland. It was opened in 1928. At that time, Suiyuan Province was experiencing a severe drought. The authorities planned to use work relief to excavate the canal, drawing water from the Yellow River for irrigation. That autumn, disaster victims were collected and engaged in excavation. By the summer of 1929, a main canal of 40 kilometers had been completed. Later, the Suiyuan provincial authorities, believing that the China International Famine Relief Commission was dedicated to construction and disaster prevention and had achieved remarkable results in managing domestic water conservancy and transportation projects, requested that it take over this project. The commission then re-surveyed and changed the original route and continued the work. By 1932, it had completed one main canal, eight branch canals, one water inlet gate at the canal entrance, two water blocking gates in the main canal, nine gate valves in the branch canals, eight large bridges in the main canal, and six wooden bridges in the branch canals, with a total expenditure of 750,000 yuan. Except for 300,000 yuan subsidized by the Suiyuan Provincial Government, the rest was allocated by the commission. At that time, the donations had been exhausted, and it was difficult to continue. Therefore, the various projects were transferred to the Suiyuan Water Conservancy Association for acceptance, while the commission still assumed the responsibility of technical guidance. It also completed one main canal outlet and four wooden bridges, and two branch canal gates. The western part of the canal project was completed. The sluice gate was opened for irrigation in the autumn of 1933, but incessant rain caused the river to rise sharply. The southern part of the canal was submerged by the Yellow River, and the northern part was eroded by mountain floods. Severe siltation occurred in the upper part of the main canal, and the irrigation goal was not achieved. The Water Conservancy Association also could not continue due to financial constraints, resulting in the suspension of the huge project, which the society deeply regretted. The commission also regretted not finishing the project. Now that the Jianghuai flood relief work has ended, it plans to carry out various construction projects to prevent drought in accordance with its usual purpose. It believes that the canal project has been suspended for a long time. If it is not quickly resumed, not only will the nearby farmland be difficult to irrigate, but also the siltation will make dredging more difficult over time. It dispatched engineer Zhang Jichun to inspect and propose a repair plan, dividing the project into two parts: repairing existing buildings and dredging silt. The estimated cost is over 100,000 yuan. It was submitted to the commission's executive committee for discussion last month. It was suggested that the project was large and costly and that the provincial authorities should cooperate fully. It was decided to allocate 10,000 yuan first to repair the original buildings. All dredging costs will be shared equally between the commission and the Suiyuan Provincial Government. Consent has been sought, and construction will begin separately after consultation.

Lu Bingsheng's Illness Confirmed; Temporary Suspension of Imprisonment Approved; Embezzlement Case Sentenced to One Year and Six Months; Appeal Rejected, Sentence Final

Lu Shaotang, a Suzhou merchant in the real estate business, and his son Lu Bingsheng, embezzled 239,000 yuan in bank notes and silver dollars while serving as president and vice president of the Bank of Communications from January 9, 1934, to May 6, 1935. Now that the case has been finalized, the First Special Court's execution office ordered Lu to report for execution of the sentence. However, Lu Bingsheng claimed to be ill and applied for a temporary suspension of execution. The court confirmed that he was indeed ill and ordered the execution to be suspended. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Shen opened the Ninth Criminal Court to continue the execution. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu also appeared in court. Lu Bingsheng, accompanied by lawyer Ye Shaoying, stated that he had not yet recovered and requested that the previous ruling be maintained and the execution suspended. This Year's Second Quarter Shanghai Industry and Commerce Change Report (Continued) (Thirty-Fifth Overview of Shanghai Industry and Commerce)

— Compiled by China Credit Bureau

B. Changes in Major Industrial and Commercial Firms in June

A. Special Industries

1. Tung Yee Trust Company Ceases Operations and Liquidates - This company was established in July of the tenth year of the Republic of China and has been in operation for fifteen years. Its fixed capital was 2.5 million national currency, with 1.36 million actually paid up. Mr. Huang Suchu, the chairman of the board, also served as general manager. It specialized in banking, trust, savings, insurance, and other businesses. Branches were established in Beiping, Hangzhou, and Suzhou, with insurance sub-bureaus and savings departments in Guangzhou, Hankou, Nanjing, and Haimen. Its daily operations focused on savings, with deposits reaching 5 million yuan at its peak. However, since the Shanghai War and the spread of economic depression throughout the country, the phenomenon of capital flight became increasingly apparent. The collapse of Tung Yee Bank in the 23rd year had a significant impact on the company due to the similarity in name. Furthermore, the market was depressed, investments in industry were difficult to recover, investments in real estate suffered from a sharp drop in land prices, and the government's unification of public bonds greatly affected securities operations. In addition, the Guangdong-Guangxi Incident led to a surge in withdrawals, reaching 100,000 to 200,000 yuan per day. As a result, deposits rapidly decreased to over 2 million yuan. The summer festival and the bank's semi-annual settlement period were approaching, and money shops were planning to withdraw loans at a rate of 3.6%, coupled with a loss of nearly 100,000 yuan due to a failed speculation in 10,000 bales of cotton yarn. By the evening of the 15th, some bills could not be cashed, leading to a lack of funds. Although the board of directors and supervisors made every effort to salvage the situation, they were ultimately unable to reverse the inevitable. The company had no choice but to declare bankruptcy on the 16th.

2. Sze Ming Bank Increases Capital - The bank's original paid-up capital was 2.25 million national currency. Last month, at the bank's 28th annual shareholders' meeting, the board of directors proposed increasing commercial shares by 1.75 million yuan, bringing the total capital to 4 million yuan. This proposal was approved by the attending shareholders in a preliminary resolution. Later, on the 21st of this month, a second general meeting was held, and the stock offering was officially approved.

3. Municipal Council Invests in Bank's Reopening - The bank was established by the Municipal Council but ceased operations after the sale of the Council's Electric Administration in the 18th year of the Republic of China. At that time, because someone purchased the Electric Administration, the proceeds from the sale were sufficient to meet all major needs, so the bank was closed. Recently, the Municipal Council board of directors, based on the recommendation of the head of the Finance Department, decided to restore the bank's operations in view of the sales of municipal public bonds this year. It began accepting deposits on June 1st. The main purpose of the bank's business is to provide citizens with various conveniences for investing in municipal bonds and also to provide the Municipal Council with a reliable source of funds. On May 5th and November 5th each year, an appropriate portion of each household's deposit will be transferred to the Municipal Council to purchase municipal bonds.

4. In the shipping industry, the closure of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Inland River Steamship Administration has also attracted much attention. The administration was directly under the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and was a joint public-private limited liability company. It had a total of twenty inland river steamships and twenty cargo ships and tugboats. Over the years, business has been poor. After the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company took back the administration's business for self-management, it made every effort to reorganize. However, it was ultimately difficult to maintain due to excessive debt, and the development of highway transportation in Jiangsu and Zhejiang in recent years has made inland river navigation practically obsolete, with little hope of recovery. Therefore, Mr. Lao Mian, who also served as manager, had no choice but to report the reorganization process and difficulties to the Ministry of Transportation for approval. The ministry ordered the cessation of operations and the sale of all ships. A shareholders' meeting was convened on the 25th of this month to report the actual situation of the closure to all shareholders.

5. In the entertainment industry, the opening of the Sun Sun Amusement Park on the 21st of this month was also an important change. The park is located from the fifth floor to the roof of the Sun Sun Company and is extremely spacious. After the Sun Sun Company completed the arrangements, it was contracted by the Xingfa Company to open for business. Therefore, although the park belongs to the Sun Sun Company, the business responsibility is entirely borne by the Xingfa Company. (To be continued)

Sports News

English Football Association Announces Two Rule Changes for This Season - Kicking Goal Kicks and Free Kicks Within the Penalty Area

The Shanghai Chinese Sports Referees Association received two rule changes announced by the English Football Association for this season yesterday. They are recorded as follows:

(1) Add a sentence to Article 1, Chapter 7: (Goal kicks must be kicked outside the penalty area line.)

"Explanation" In the past, it was customary for defenders to pass the ball to the goalkeeper for a goal kick. The current rule stipulates that only one player is allowed to kick the ball directly out of the penalty area. If the ball fails to be kicked out of the penalty area, the referee will order a retake. However, the kicker is not allowed to kick the ball twice. Violators will be penalized with a free kick.

(2) Add two sentences to Article 1, Chapter 10: When a free kick is awarded within the penalty area, the penalized team's players must defend on the goal line.

"Explanation" In the past, players on the penalized team could form a wall to defend freely. The current rule stipulates that they are only allowed to make this defensive formation on the goal line.

Shanghai National Martial Arts Center Adds Sanda and Piercing Classes

The Shanghai National Martial Arts Center has been established for eight years and has been committed to the martial arts movement, sparing no effort. The center recently added Sanda and Piercing classes, as they are practical techniques for unarmed combat and combat situations. The classes are scheduled to be held every Saturday and Sunday from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM at the fifth training ground in the Tianhou Palace. They will be taught by national martial arts masters Tong Zhongyi, Jin Yunting, Zhao Shouchun, Ma Wanlong, and Ma Hanzhang. Classes are scheduled to start today (September 5th). It is also learned that the center is currently soliciting membership fees for half a year, with two types: special (six yuan) and ordinary (four yuan). Brochures are printed and can be requested by mail from the main center at Xinhe River, Minguo Road. It is reported that the number of people signing up has been very enthusiastic recently.

Account of Our Country's Athletes Participating in the Expedition (Eleventh Letter) Special Correspondent Feng Youzhen from the Central News Agency

(5) (3) Basketball Team Unsuccessful - Initial Battle Lost to Japan

The seventh day of the Games marked the start of the first week of basketball competition, with a total of nine matches. In addition, there was a match between the United States and Spain. However, Spain did not participate in the Games. A match between the Czech Republic and Hungary also resulted in Hungary's forfeit, and the Philippines had a bye. All advanced to the second week without effort.

Of the nine matches, the match between China and Japan attracted the most interest from the audience. More than 2,000 people went to watch, which was very different from the cold and quiet atmosphere of other matches.

On our country's side, whether they were delegation staff or athletes, or students studying in Europe, everyone was extremely concerned about the outcome of this match. One reason was that all other sports had failed, and only basketball had hope of progress. The other reason was that everyone hoped to beat the Japanese basketball team, which had always been defeated by us, in front of the Europeans. Therefore, almost all Chinese people in Berlin, from Dean Dai and Ambassador Cheng onwards, were mobilized. Students studying in Germany and students studying in other European countries who came to Berlin to visit the Games organized a cheering squad to cheer on the team. They cheered and shouted very neatly on the field, which was in stark contrast to the Japanese side, which only had one person holding a national flag and singing a solo act. However, the result of the match was that we were defeated by Japan, and the defeat was very惨 (can3 - tragic, miserable), which was like pouring a bucket of cold water over everyone's heads. Everyone was discouraged and dejected. The players, in particular, suffered a great blow. After the match, they were all stunned and, when they returned to the Olympic Village, cried bitterly and were filled with sadness. The stimulus given to everyone by this competition was exceptionally tragic. I think when the reporter broadcasted the situation to the country by radio during the competition, the listeners must have been very angry as well. The biggest reason for the failure was that everyone took the outcome of this competition too seriously. The compatriots in Berlin all had the mentality that they could only win and not lose. However, the importance of winning and losing was too great, which had too much impact on the players' mood. Since the order of the matches was drawn on the 27th of last month, the members of the basketball team had been worried about the outcome of this match almost every day. Half of the worry was due to external stimuli, and half was due to internal feelings. Therefore, when they went to the field to compete, everyone's mood was unusually tense, and their nerves were unusually excited. As a result of the tension and excitement, the formation was very chaotic, and their skills were completely abnormal. After Mu Zuoyun opened the scoring under the basket, the Japanese side had four consecutive fouls. Because they were too eager to win and their mood was chaotic, they did not score even once. The Japanese took advantage of the free throw opportunity and scored two out of two, and then scored another point with a throw and a free throw, taking the lead with a score of 5-2. Our team members became even more disoriented as a result. If everyone could have fought calmly and not missed the free throw opportunities, then we would have taken the lead with a score of 6-0 at the beginning, and the momentum would have been completely different. The competition would have become a completely different situation. In total, our team had 13 free throws in the whole match, but only scored three. The Japanese side only missed six out of 17 free throws. The situation is also conceivable. Secondly, the progress of the Japanese side's basketball skills cannot be ignored. They adopted a steady and methodical strategy, with no fancy moves at all, but very solid. When attacking, they found a gap and drilled in like mercury. When defending, the positions were arranged very tightly, and no defects were easily revealed. Their team this time is not comparable to the team at the last Far Eastern Games. We should learn from their spirit of hard training and striving for progress. Coach Dong Shouyi was seriously ill and went to the hospital. There was no one to guide the team during the competition. Captain Wang Yuzeng had just recovered from a minor illness and was not in good physical condition. The outcome of the competition was somewhat affected.

Hard Work in the First Half

After the opening, the Japanese team once shot at our basket but missed. Our team immediately took the offensive, passing the ball several times. Mu Zuoyun leaped into the air under the basket, broke the net, and opened the scoring. The whole audience cheered and the momentum was full. The Japanese fought back desperately, and their movements were inevitably rough, committing four fouls in a row. Our side let them off lightly. Li Shaotang violated military law, and the Japanese side did not hesitate to score each time. Yokoyama, who was small but courageous and lively, tried his hand at the right corner and hit the bullseye. He then followed up with a free throw, taking the lead with a score of 5-2. Mu Zuoyun and Wang Yuzeng were unwilling to submit and broke through the basket one after another, taking the lead again with a score of 6-5. The Japanese scored again with a free throw, and we fell behind again with a score of 7-6. After that, the Japanese played steadily and advanced by taking advantage of weaknesses, adding eight points in a row. Our side was at a loss. Although Mu and Wang each scored a goal, we still lost the first half with a score of 15-10.

Total Defeat in the Second Half

After resting and fighting again, the Japanese scored again with a free throw. After Xiao Mu fought back with a goal, Li Shaotang's sentence expired and he announced his resignation. Wang Shixuan took the stage and became a general, but his power was not reduced. The Japanese three forwards suddenly became active, scoring twice and making a free throw, taking a remote lead with a score of 20-10. Shen Yugong replaced Mu Zuoyun and gave a warning shot. Wang Yuzeng scored the first free throw, chasing the score to 20-15, which seemed to be a turning point. However, it was a flash in the pan. The good times did not last long. After the Japanese added eight points in a row, Shen Yugong finally scored two points with a free throw. With not much time left, the Japanese adopted a delaying tactic. Our army fought desperately, but instead revealed gaps and gave away five more points. Wang Yuzeng made a long shot, and the Japanese returned the favor in the same way. The game ended, and our side suffered a惨 (can3 - tragic, miserable) defeat with a score of 35-19.

Ministry of Education Compiles Detailed Elementary School Physical Education Teaching Outline

Ministry Orders Elementary School Physical Education Teachers to Adopt

In view of the fact that there has never been a uniform teaching material for physical education in elementary schools across the country, the Ministry of Education has specially invited experts to compile a detailed elementary school physical education teaching outline. The entire book is 100,000 words long and is divided into four thick volumes. The first volume is a general preface and instructions for operation items, instructing elementary school physical education teachers on teaching methods, curriculum arrangement methods, and the distribution and utilization methods of teaching materials. The second volume is the game category, which lists hundreds of various game teaching materials, divided into categories such as competition, chase and escape, stories, and ball games. Each type of game has distinctions for senior, middle, and junior grades. The third volume is the rhythmic activity category, which is divided into dance and singing games. There are hundreds of teaching materials. In addition to the descriptive text, all kinds of dances are accompanied by musical scores. The fourth volume is gymnastics and sports. The gymnastics teaching materials list various preparatory steps and team formations. The teaching materials for Tai Chi exercises are also fully adopted. The book has been ordered by the Ministry of Education to be adopted and tested by all elementary school physical education teachers starting from this autumn. It has been entrusted to the Qinfen Bookstore at 277 Sima Road, Shanghai, for distribution. The entire four volumes cost 1.4 yuan, with an additional 5 cents for postage for out-of-town areas and an additional 8 cents for registration.

University Graduates' Employment Training - Registration Reaches 4,000 People - Exceeding the Original Quota by 3,000, Including More Than 200 Students Returning from Abroad

(Nanjing, 4th) Registration for the employment guidance class for graduates of colleges and universities closed on the 31st of last month. Statistics show that the number of applicants is 4,000, including more than 200 students returning from abroad. The total number has exceeded the original quota of 3,000 by more than 1,000. The Ministry of Education has requested that the Executive Yuan, the actual ministries, the Central Political School, and the Academic Advisory Council each send two representatives to form a qualification review committee. The meeting will be established next week, which is set up by the Ministry of Education.
