Shanghai Bar Association: Compilation and Printing of Continued Laws and Regulations

The third collection of the "Continued Compilation of Current Laws and Regulations of the National Government," compiled and printed by the Shanghai Bar Association, has now been published. It includes various laws and regulations: (1) Provisional Regulations on the Organization of County Judicial Offices; (2) Supplementary Regulations on Litigation Handled by County Judicial Offices; (3) Provisional Regulations on Criminal Case Review by County Judicial Offices; (4) Implementation Measures for Postal Delivery of Litigation Documents; (5) Rules for Penalties and Enforcement by Judicial Organs Under the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations; (6) Amendment to Eleven Articles of the Provisional Regulations on the Transfer of Prisoners for Land Reclamation; (7) Provisional Notarization Rules; (8) Detailed Rules for the Implementation of Provisional Notarization Rules; (9) Rules on Notarization Fees; (10) Provisional Regulations on Punishing Opium Suppression Crimes; (11) Provisional Regulations on Punishing Drug Suppression Crimes; (12) Organizational Regulations of the National Government Military Commission's General Opium Suppression Association; (13) General Rules on the Organization of Opium Suppression Committees in Provinces, Cities, and Counties; (14) Litigation Instructions; (15) Matters Requiring Attention in Handling Criminal Litigation Cases; (16) Revised Matters Requiring Attention in Handling Civil Litigation Cases; (17) Rules for Lawyers to Inspect Case Files; (18) Various laws and regulations, such as the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works' Schedule of Fees for Appraising Real Estate. This is a non-commercial item, and all members can receive a complimentary copy, it is said.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The Shandong area is overcast with showers and strong tornadoes due to a hurricane passing through the Yellow Sea, moving north and northeast. The Yellow River basin has localized showers with variable winds. The Yangtze River basin is cloudy and hot with southeasterly to southwesterly winds. The East China Sea is cloudy with strong southeasterly winds. A small hurricane southwest of Taiwan will continue to move northwest. At 6:00 AM, its center was located within approximately 60 miles of 21 degrees north latitude and 121 degrees east longitude. The wind force is unknown. The center of the first hurricane was located within approximately 60 miles of 36 degrees north latitude and 122 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, moving north with strong winds. Furthermore, in the 24 hours prior to 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was a maximum of 92.5 and a minimum of 73.8. On the same day last year, the maximum was 86.9 and the minimum was 73.4.

Letter

To the Editor:

I recently read a news item in the local news column of your newspaper on August 28 concerning a labor dispute at the China Battery Factory. The report stated that Zhu Yichen ganged up with Yang Ziliang, Huang Chenglin, and others to kidnap Xiao Shunquan and illegally detain him in room 78 of the Dahua Hotel at Xixin Bridge, threatening Xiao Shunquan to return to Yangzhou immediately and not work in Shanghai. Zhu did not express anything, and he was detained without freedom, etc. Upon investigation, our factory previously had a dispute due to discord among the workers, which has been mediated and resolved. The news reported above is not entirely consistent with the facts and is likely based on inaccurate rumors. We are concerned about misunderstandings from all sectors. Therefore, we have specially prepared this letter to clarify and request your newspaper to correct it. Please forward this to the Editor of Shen Bao.

Sincerely,

Hu Guoguang, Manager of China Battery Factory

For the Adjustment of the Chinese Buddhist Association: A Notice to Monks and Nuns Nationwide (Continued). By Zhang Tinghao. (4) Regulations on Annual Donations

Annual donations are, in a sense, not a new addition. In January of last year, the Chinese Buddhist Association itself had already formulated a set of rules for temples to establish charitable and public welfare undertakings, which were submitted to the Ministry of Interior for record. However, because the rules were mostly formulated by abbots of large monasteries with higher incomes, the percentage was set high for temples and nunneries with lower incomes, and conversely, low for temples and nunneries with higher incomes. It should be known that the majority of temples and nunneries nationwide have lower incomes. According to the percentage set by those rules, those with an income of one hundred yuan donate one percent. Assuming that each such temple has three resident monks, an income of one hundred yuan is already very difficult to maintain the clothing and food of three people throughout the year, but they still have to donate one percent. While those with an income of tens of thousands of yuan, whose numbers may not increase proportionally, and whose expenses, if not abused, may not particularly increase, donate the same as those with an income of one thousand yuan, which is only five percent. Isn't this clearly showing favoritism and being too unfair? Monks and nuns practicing asceticism and self-discipline are originally their duty, but they cannot completely disregard their livelihoods. Moreover, if there is unequal treatment among monks and nuns, it further violates the Buddhist doctrine of equality. Compared with the original rules, the draft charter reduces the percentage for those with lower incomes and appropriately increases the percentage for those with higher incomes, based solely on facts and seeking fairness. Moreover, the purpose of the donations is to conduct education and charitable public welfare undertakings. If monks and nuns understand the Buddhist spirit of altruism, they should not oppose it against their conscience.

Since I welcome monks and nuns nationwide to express their opinions on the draft charter as much as possible, as long as the reasons are sufficient, the opinions of opponents can certainly be accommodated. However, regarding the recent letter from the current Standing Council of the Chinese Buddhist Association to all directors and supervisors for distributing research on the draft charter I proposed, the point about abolishing provincial associations and adopting a two-level system was clearly advocated by the previous council of the association. Before the 7th National Congress, it was submitted to the former Central People's Movement Committee to request modification. The former People's Movement Committee listed the points to be considered and ordered further research. After the association replied, explaining in detail, the former People's Movement Committee only temporarily approved it for record after the 7th National Congress. But the letter says, "Following the instructions of the Central Government to improve, the Buddhist associations of each province were abolished," pushing the proposal to abolish provincial Buddhist associations onto the Central Government. And in the "Hai Chao" Volume 17, No. 7, such as the articles "Jinshan Conference and Central Opinions," "Regarding the Chinese Buddhist Association Incident," and "Reviewing the Central Amendment Draft from the History of the Chinese Buddhist Association," it is repeatedly said that the Central Civil Training Department sent personnel to participate in guiding the Jinshan Conference, and the Chinese Buddhist Association is currently suspended from activities. According to the facts, Director Wu of the Civil Training Department went to Zhenjiang clearly to stop the meeting, not to guide the meeting. The Civil Training Department and the Ministry of Interior have also not suspended the activities of the Chinese Buddhist Association. These various cunning means of deliberately obliterating the facts and deceiving themselves not only intend to lie to monks and nuns nationwide, but are simply disregarding the Central Government. "Falsehood" is one of the Buddhist precepts. Since you have taken the pure precepts of a Buddhist, why imitate the sinister and cunning behavior of politicians? How can you face Shakyamuni? How can you face the monks and nuns nationwide? Buddha emphasizes repentance. Therefore, I hope that those Buddhists who stubbornly hold onto their ego, still want to fight openly and secretly, and are willing to violate precepts and ruin conduct, losing their true faith, will quickly and sincerely repent and no longer have words and deeds that violate Buddhist law, but work together to seek the revival of Chinese Buddhism.

For example, a school was originally very corrupt and had no discipline. Once the education authorities formulated some measures and strictly ordered rectification, at first, in addition to one or two teachers who truly worked for education, of course, not only would the students complain endlessly, but I am afraid that even the teachers who were just filling positions would not feel greatly inconvenienced. However, if the teachers and students can resolve to comply and implement it for a slightly longer period, the school's academic atmosphere will improve, and the students' studies will progress. As a result, the reputation and practical benefits will still be enjoyed by the entire school of teachers and students. This time, I was ordered to adjust the Chinese Buddhist Association and draft the charter of the Buddhist Association. The situation is really similar to this. Abbots and monks and nuns nationwide, do you want the Buddhist Association to be permanently corrupt, or do you hope for rectification?

Yarn and Cotton: The Storm Caused Little Damage, Cotton Prices Fell Sharply, Fortunately, Large Traders Covered Short Positions, Leading to a Drop of Only Six or Seven Jiao

The cotton market had previously rebounded due to excitement about the impending hurricane. However, US cotton suddenly reversed from rising to falling, and the hurricane also passed peacefully. There were no reports of any damage to the cotton-producing areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. As a result, sentiment rapidly declined, and market prices fell sharply. However, Changhe and others substantially covered their short positions, amounting to a huge sum of nearly 30,000 bales, which helped to maintain market prices.

Changhe Substantially Covered Short Positions

The spot cotton market opened in the morning with a sudden fall in US cotton, which had been rising for several days, due to favorable weather conditions. At the same time, the weather in this city was clear, the hurricane had passed, and it had not affected important cotton-producing areas. The new cotton harvest was not expected to be affected in any way. Sentiment was unanimously bearish, and there was a strong selling trend in the market. Prices for near-term contracts fell sharply by seven or eight jiao, while prices for far-term contracts fell by five or six jiao. Acute gonorrhea is very painful; chronic gonorrhea has deep viral roots.

Women's Special Publication

New and Old Perspectives on Chinese Women

— Gang

Chinese women have been oppressed by men since ancient times, and this has become a common practice. Since the May Fourth Movement, although some educated women have been striving for liberation, importing new ideas and trends from Europe and the West, very few truly understand and appreciate them. As for old-fashioned women, they naturally do not understand what learning and thought are, blindly clinging to the so-called three obediences and four virtues, which is indeed a great pity. But they each have their strengths and weaknesses, with their own advantages and disadvantages!

Regarding knowledge, new women undoubtedly have the upper hand. Having received education—whether general or higher education—they at least understand some common sense about family and society and will not believe in superstitions and unscientific ideas. Furthermore, they excel in fine arts, crafts, and social skills. Therefore, they also feel a strong interest in life. Old-fashioned women are different: because they have not attended school, their knowledge and experience are limited, so they are unaccustomed to new sounds (like music) and sights (like art). They do not know how big the Earth is; a county town or a city is their world. This is indeed the biggest shortcoming of old-fashioned women, and the main reason why they cannot keep pace with women around the world.

Regarding household management, on the surface, it seems that new-style women are more knowledgeable, but in practice, old-fashioned women are more capable of managing things with ease. This is not surprising because educated women are required to pursue academic progress on the one hand, and take care of household chores on the other, so they naturally become neglectful and lack focus. Moreover, having come from schools, they have very little practical experience once they become housewives. Old-fashioned women are trained from childhood and are more able to endure hardship. They regard household management as their inherent duty and do not feel disgusted. Apart from this, they have no other thoughts in their minds.

Divorce is a very serious issue in modern society. The reason is mostly due to the influence of a bad environment. The reason why old-fashioned women do not have this problem is partly because they lack the ability and intellectual tools, and partly because their desires are easily satisfied, as long as their husbands can provide them with food and clothing, they consider themselves happy, unlike new women who are good at being demanding. Such blind obedience allows men to abuse them at will, and new women, being oppressed under strong authority, are certainly unwilling to submit. However, it is also not commendable for new women to be arrogant and frivolous, to look down on others, and to declare divorce with a little superficial knowledge.

Comparing the above items, we can see the general situation of modern new and old women. It is hoped that they will develop their strengths and overcome their weaknesses, which would be the blessing of the women's world!

Chinese Women in a Time of Turmoil

— Zhou Xian

Chinese women, whose new foundations are not yet fully stable and whose old structures have been largely destroyed, can be said to be in the most dangerous position in this time of turmoil. This is the criticism of Chinese women published by Mrs. Hua Lei Si, who lived in China for seventeen years and recently returned to England, in the British magazine Red Star. The title of this article is "Chinese Women in a Time of Turmoil."

She said that although Chinese women have had more than ten years of history since liberation, it is naturally not enough to completely transform the solid position of women for three thousand years in just over ten years. Therefore, Chinese women are currently only just raising the curtain on the new women's movement. But unfortunately, Chinese women have encountered a major setback in this first act. — This setback can also be said to be that Chinese women themselves have gone astray. Because the slogans of the liberation movement for Chinese women are "social openness," "freedom of occupation," and "equal opportunities," but the effect of these slogans has completely turned into a tool for marriage. When love matures, "social interaction," "occupation," "opportunity,"... are all automatically abandoned. Although this phenomenon is undoubtedly due to the marriage system and the patriarchal society of China for three thousand years being too firmly rooted, and the general public regards the issue of marriage as the most important thing above all else, and this kind of legacy is still traditionally inherited, the naivety of the Chinese education on "men and women issues" cannot be blamed. Because the Chinese concept of chastity still preserves the畸形 habits of three thousand years, and has not been improved at all due to the emerging women's movement. This is the most dangerous and sad position in which Chinese women find themselves in this time of turmoil.

Mrs. Hua Lei Si quoted a story witnessed in China. She said that a Chinese lady worked very hard for the liberation movement of Chinese women. She had received a considerable education, and she had also worked in a certain commercial institution. In 1927, she married a university student because of love. After marriage, she immediately resigned from her job because her husband was enough to maintain her life. At the same time, she also disappeared from social circles because she was afraid that her husband would suspect her of having romantic actions. After a year, she was abandoned by her husband because he discovered a secret of hers before marriage. Although she received alimony in 1929 and formally divorced, her reputation and status were greatly damaged. Her parents, brothers, and even her closest sister broke off contact with her. At the same time, she also felt that she was a woman with extremely deep sins, and everything seemed to be over. Sadness and depression pressed on her entire soul. In 1931, her divorced husband married another woman, but she went crazy in 1932. She lived in the hospital for two years and finally died in 1934. When she first divorced, Mrs. Hua Lei Si tried her best to guide and comfort her, but she insisted on the theory of status and environment, and did not have the courage to fight for status and environment, and finally sacrificed everything.

What Mrs. Hua Lei Si said is only a corner of the women's liberation movement. In reality, the traps on the road to liberation are densely arranged. — I feel that in this turbulent period, if Chinese women cannot have sufficient cultivation and understanding in the two aspects of education and thought, and rashly engage in it, compared with standing on an unstable new foundation, the danger is even greater!

— Jun Peng

- Female Police Needed -

Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau has recruited many female police officers, which some people may find strange. In fact, it is a very ordinary thing in foreign countries, but in China, it is the first time ever. We have always had a saying: "Good people don't become soldiers, good iron isn't used to make nails." But looking at the number of applicants this time, there are as many as two hundred people, most of whom are high school graduates, junior college graduates, and junior high school graduates, followed by elementary school graduates. Such enthusiasm is really beyond the expectations of ordinary people. Isn't it breaking our deeply rooted bad ideas?

We must know that China is in danger of being invaded by powerful neighbors day and night. No matter where or when, we are in a state of emergency. Everyone should arm themselves to defend the country. If something happens to the country in the future, who do you want to maintain social order? Then, we will naturally need our trained female police officers to take responsibility for maintaining local order. Since China is now in a state of emergency, preparations for self-rescue must be carried out actively. Hey! Look: During the European War, almost all the able-bodied men in Germany went to war. Social security relied on many female police officers to be responsible for maintaining order just like usual. In this way, are female police officers not needed?

Finally, I hope that all provinces and cities across the country have the need to recruit female police officers. If something happens to the four families, there will be many female police officers who will be responsible for social security. The military and police on the front line will no longer have to worry about social security in the rear, so they can not be divided into combat strength. China's need for female police officers goes without saying. I hope the authorities will work hard to promote it, and women will enthusiastically apply for the responsibility of being female police officers in times of emergency.

Because the Spanish royalists and right-wing republicans joined forces to fight against the left-wing government, Spain fell into a state of unrest. Recently, several fierce battles have taken place, which aroused my interest in the new women in Spain who are in the process of liberation.

London Women's Book Club

The East End of London established a new "Housewives' Book Club" this spring. The purpose of the club is that general housewives are burdened by housework every day, and some do not read a book all year round. This is not enough for their own intellectual nourishment, and there is a risk of regressing or falling behind day by day. At the same time, it is natural that it cannot but give a considerable response to the education of children. Therefore, this housewives' book club came into being. To join this housewives' book club, the annual membership fee is five pounds. The club lends a famous book every ten days or half a month, and limits how many days to finish reading it. (Generally, the standard is to study for one and a half to two hours every day.) After reading, they must also make a report, stating their thoughts after reading. This is tantamount to a kind of forced reading method, so that the housewives who join the club cannot but take time to read every day, and the method is very good. It is heard that there are now about two thousand people who have joined. Among them, there are two hundred members who live far away in South Africa, North America, Shanghai, Australia, and various parts of Europe.

Special Report from This Newspaper

Medical Doctor Liu Jianqiu Discusses Family Hygiene

— Ji Ping

Where does the starting point of a happy new family lie? Some people say: Having money satisfies everything, and some people say: Having excellent children makes a family happy. This statement has considerable truth, but money is not necessarily the happiness of a family. Sometimes money is the root of evil, causing dark and terrifying events. It can be seen that surplus money is unreliable. I believe that a healthy life is the starting point of happiness and well-being. In any family, if men, women, old and young, injure or fall ill, spending their days with medicine, this is the most painful thing. On the contrary, if everyone in the family is strong and healthy, those who work hard, those who study diligently, and work together to develop their careers, I feel that this family is the happiest. Speaking of this problem, it can be said to be the most difficult to handle. Regardless of parents and children, everyone must pay attention to cleanliness and hygiene. Everyone can say this, but how to do it? I am afraid that it cannot be done without the guidance of a doctor. The other day, I discussed these issues with a female doctor - Dr. Liu Jianqiu. She is from Pixian County, Jiangsu Province, and a graduate of the first class of Jinling Women's University. She studied in the United States for six years and obtained a medical doctorate from the University of Michigan. In the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, she returned to China and served as the director of obstetrics and gynecology at the Ximen Women's and Children's Hospital in Shanghai, Dinghai Hospital, and Hangzhou Municipal Hospital. Since the eighteenth year, she has served as the medical director of Renhe Hospital and the dean of the Senior Midwifery School. With more than ten years of experience, her contributions to medicine are naturally great. Here, her words are recorded for the reference of general housewives.

The first point is the perception of medicine: Although I am a doctor myself, I do not want to talk about the medical career, because Chinese people are too superstitious and lack medical knowledge, and do not have a thorough understanding and recognition of new medicine. When a person gets sick and asks a doctor, they often do not listen to the doctor's instructions. When something goes wrong, they complain that the doctor is not responsible enough. This is such an injustice! On the doctor's side, few can study the patient's psychology. The lack of mutual consideration is also a cause of failure. New medicine is still in its infancy in China. Except for cities, rural areas have not yet received the benefits of new medicine. There are probably several reasons: (1) There are too few new doctors, not enough to distribute; (2) The life in the interior is extremely difficult and transportation is difficult. Even if there are doctors, patients cannot afford to seek medical treatment from afar; (3) Farmers do not accumulate wealth easily and naturally value money very much. They do not know the price of Western medicine. For example, if a medicine is worth five yuan, they want it for three yuan, and they cannot wait for the medical expenses to be completely free. But how can this be done in reality? Therefore, I believe that Chinese society must use the power of politics to promote public health in rural areas, reward scientific new medicine, and change people's psychology. Then the future of new medicine will be promising.

The second point is women's hygiene: The two words hygiene are not easy to talk about. Only with money can we talk about hygiene. You think of the four basic needs of life, clothing, food, shelter and transportation, all of which require sufficient economy to be considered? Now most people's lives are not easy to maintain, so where can we talk about hygiene? This is the case in cities, and it goes without saying in rural areas. Hygiene should be paid attention to by both men and women. However, Chinese women have been subjected to all kinds of unequal shackles for thousands of years, living a life like cattle and horses. How can they talk about hygiene? Now that the women's world has opened its mind and is in a better position, they know that hygiene must be paid attention to. The structure of a woman's body is very different from that of a man's, so she cannot endure labor as long as a man. This is a natural disadvantage. Furthermore, foot binding and breast binding are the most painful things for women. However, in rural areas in the interior, these customs have not been completely eradicated. This kind of bad custom causes lifelong pain to women. In essence, it is more tragic than murder. This is the most unfortunate and unhygienic thing for women. I hope the local authorities will seriously ban it. Women's hygiene is very simple. I think what is more important than this is the happiness of the family. A family should be united in love and understanding. However, the most common problem now is that couples do not care about each other and have no love to speak of. Some couples are at odds due to economic poverty, which is most unfortunate. They should understand each other more when they are poorer, so that there is a possibility of improving their lives.

The third is the common sense of family hygiene: The same family has many different things in cities and rural areas. In daily life, I think rural areas are much more beautiful than cities. For example, although rural people live in thatched houses, the surrounding air is fresh and the sunlight is abundant. Children receive more than ten hours of sunlight every day, while urban residents live in pigeon-shed-like houses, where sunlight is not easy to reach. Eating is the most important thing for a family's nutrition. Farmers have fresh fruits and vegetables, which are the richest in vitamins, while urban people usually eat food that is not very fresh. Family hygiene is originally based on diet, followed by housing and clothing, but the habits of our people are the opposite. It is common to see that many children in Shanghai suffer from beriberi and rickets (i.e., osteomalacia). What is the child like? Adults can imagine. This is evidence that the diet is unhygienic. If a housewife does not pay attention to diet first, how can she talk about raising children?

The fourth is children's hygiene: Children should be allowed to develop naturally, and too much restraint will not work. However, cleanliness is of course the first priority for everything they need in life. Unfortunately, most families do not pay attention to cleanliness. It is best to keep children away from bacteria. However, once they encounter bacteria, they get sick, just like the flowers and plants in the greenhouse. They usually do not see sunlight, and they wither as soon as they see sunlight. On the other hand, children who adapt to the natural environment have the ability to resist bacteria, but the mortality rate of the latter is higher than that of the former. Therefore, the compromise is that children should not be too restrained or allowed to be too casual. Cleanliness and hygiene must be paid attention to. Middle and upper-class families in cities like to burn strong electric lights. When children sleep, the electric lights are still bright. They do not know that strong electric lights are harmful to children's eyesight and even to their nerves, and there is a risk of mental disorder. These cannot be taken lightly.

Ms. Liu Jianqiu

Sister Hui (Part 2)

— Yin

Luckily, Xi-sheng had seen this brother-in-law once when his sister got married, otherwise he would have really suspected he had come to the wrong place; however, although he recognized the man, seeing his grand demeanor and his loud voice, Xi-sheng was stunned and wondered what to do. He truly regretted not braving a beating and staying at his uncle's house instead of coming out. Seeing him lower his head and not say a word, Chen Er-shao-ye naturally grew impatient waiting, and barked at him as if dealing with a beggar: "Your sister is out. Come back another day!"

After saying these words, as if he had fulfilled his responsibility as a brother-in-law, he turned around and went back inside. Xi-sheng, however, couldn't follow him in. Seeing the two servants beside him glaring at him fiercely, how could he dare to linger? He hurriedly heaved up the large bundle and backed out of the door. By the time he reached the last step of the stone stairs, tears were already hanging on the corners of his mouth.

When he set out from the countryside, his uncle was kind enough to give him a bowl of cold porridge before he left. But after walking so far, the bowl of cold porridge had long been used up. His stomach was rumbling with hunger, and his legs unknowingly grew weak. He sat down on the doorstep of a incense and candle shop to the left of the Chen family, unable to walk any further. Fortunately, the people in the shop didn't chase him away, allowing him to stay there alone.

After a long while, three rickshaws came from the west side of the street. One of the three women sitting in the rickshaws seemed very familiar to Xi-sheng. Could it be Sister Hui? But she wasn't so beautiful before! Then he heard her speak, and it really was Sister Hui. Xi-sheng couldn't help but get excited. He was about to step forward, but then he didn't dare. He was afraid she would be like her brother-in-law. Besides, he and Sister Hui had always argued since childhood. Maybe she would be even less willing to take him in than her brother-in-law! So he didn't have the courage. He watched helplessly as she helped an old lady out of the rickshaw, paid the fare, and walked into the Chen family's gate with a female servant carrying a baby. Xi-sheng's eyes followed her all the way in, but in the end, he didn't have the courage to call out.

Sister Hui is back now. Should he try going in again? Xi-sheng pondered this question for a long time, but couldn't make a decision. Moreover, his stomach couldn't go a day without food! The problem of survival trapped this seventeen-year-old country boy. In the end, he felt the best course of action was to quickly go back to the countryside, falsely claim that his brother-in-law's family had moved, and he couldn't find them, and then mooch off his uncle for a while longer. He was almost about to stand up and leave when the servant who had glanced at him from the Chen family's gate suddenly came out, craning his neck and looking around as if looking for someone. Then he saw Xi-sheng and hurried over to ask:

"Are you the young master from the countryside?"

Xi-sheng didn't know if he was a young master or not, but he simply replied, "I'm from the countryside." The servant then readily picked up the bundle for him and led him back into the Chen family. Xi-sheng thought that his brother-in-law must have seen his sister return, so he sent someone to find him. But when he entered, he saw that the person standing in front of the hall was not the fierce brother-in-law, but Sister Hui, who he had always argued with since childhood!

As soon as they met, the siblings couldn't help but cry. The great love between siblings, in the context of a vast disparity in wealth, was finally fully expressed.

Supplement to the Shanghai Shenbao

Ling Shu and Su Wen (The Spiritual Pivot and Simple Questions)

— Answered by Dr. Liu Xinbai

What You Need to Know When Asking About Illnesses

1. Letters must be written in plain language.

2. Do not write about "wind," "cold," "fire," or "dampness." Do not use vague "disease names" that are difficult to grasp and lack specific meaning.

3. Write about the symptoms, the more detailed the better.

4. Please include a stamp with your letter. Out-of-town letters require a five-cent stamp, and local letters require a two-cent stamp. Letters that I deem to have no value for publication, or those that patients do not wish to be published, will be answered directly by mail.

5. Please write your detailed address clearly.

6. Send letters to my clinic, 1108 Qinyuan Village, Xinza Road, Shanghai.

7. There is no charge for asking about illnesses.

8. If you are asking about two illnesses in one letter, or several aspects of one illness—for example, cause, symptoms, diagnosis, prognosis, treatment—please use numbers to indicate them.

9. Questions are limited to internal medicine, dermatology, and venereology.

Swollen and Painful Limbs

No. 1 Mr. Ren Xingwu of Sitiao Lane, Nanjing, asks: My body has always been healthy, and I have not been ill for eighteen years. But twenty days ago, I suddenly developed a fever, and at the same time, my left elbow, wrist, knee, ankle, and other places became hot, red, and swollen. The pain was so severe that it went straight to my heart. I consulted a venereal disease doctor, who said it was arthritis caused by gonorrhea. I have always been clean and self-disciplined and have never been involved in any promiscuous activities. Later, I took "Salvarsan" and "Aspirin," etc., and recovered completely in more than ten days. But a few days after recovering, it flared up again, even worse than before. Please tell me: (1) Is this "gonorrheal arthritis?" (2) Can this disease occur even if one has never been promiscuous? (3) If so, what kind of treatment is best? Can "Salvarsan" and "Aspirin" be taken? (4) In addition to the fever, I also feel depressed. Is this because "fire is attacking internally?" (1) It is probably not "gonorrheal arthritis" but "acute polyarthritic rheumatism." This disease is called "Luma Zhisi" in Japanese and "Rheumatic Fever" in English. There are three types: single-cycle, multi-cycle, and persistent. Your condition probably belongs to the multi-cycle type. (2) No. (3) "Salvarsan" and "Aspirin" are effective for rheumatism, but since you have already consulted a doctor, the results of an examination are more reliable than asking by mail. It is best to consult a reliable doctor again. The most effective drug for rheumatism is "SinoPhAn," which can be injected or taken orally. (4) The word "fire" is too metaphysical. Please do not use this kind of wording in future correspondence. Rheumatic fever can easily cause myocarditis. The depression in your chest is highly suggestive of myocarditis. This disease can cause valvular insufficiency as a sequela. It is best to seek treatment as soon as possible.

After answering, I feel there are still points you should pay attention to, namely: (1) Rest. It is best to be absolutely quiet, lie in bed, and not move. Wrap the affected area with cotton (dry or wet). (2) Diet should consist of liquids, milk, soft-boiled eggs, porridge, and soup. (3) Drink plenty of ice water. You can drink five or six thermos bottles (one pound each) every day. (4) It is best to be hospitalized.

Strange Child's Illness

No. 2 Mr. Ta Bin of Rongxian Hutong, Beijing, asks: I have a child who is five years old this year (actually four years old). He has not grown at all since he was born. He also has no teeth. Only this year has he grown two and a half teeth, one is the fourth left incisor, and one is the third right incisor in the lower row. The reason I say half is because they are uneven and don't look like teeth at all. He still can't walk. Even if an adult helps him walk, he walks crookedly and doesn't look like he's walking at all. His bones are very thin, as if there is no flesh between his skin and bones. But he still eats a lot. Some time ago, because his belly was big, I consulted a famous doctor specializing in treating bloating, but he couldn't say what was wrong, and the medicine didn't work. I heard that you are very knowledgeable. I don't know if this kind of disease can be cured.

Answer: Mr. Ta, you flatter me. Your letter is so clear and understandable. It is absolutely unique among the letters I receive every day. Your son's illness is so strange (actually not strange at all; there are no strange things in the world, Mr. Ta has just rarely heard of them), that it has aroused great interest in us. I am very willing to give you a detailed answer. I am afraid that you will not be able to see the supplement in Beijing, so I will send you another copy. Have you heard of the name "rickets?" Your son has this disease. The cause of this disease is a lack of "Vitamin " and " ". The symptoms are unnecessary to say, they are just like what you said. You certainly hope to cure him. Please buy "Hailimin" for him to eat. After eating it, you will feel strange, "Oh! Can this disease also be cured?" It is even better to take "Sinocalcin" at the same time to supplement the calcium in the body.

Breathing Difficulties

No. 3 Mr. Li Jianhun asks: I am eighteen years old this year. My mother, aunt, uncle, and aunt all died of tuberculosis. I have been malnourished since I was a child, have a poor memory, cough, and get out of breath after walking a few steps. I eat very little, am very thin, and my hands and feet are cold all year round. All of this doesn't matter. The most painful thing is that my breathing is not smooth. It occurs every three or four months. When it happens, I can't sit or stand still, and I don't know whether to cry or laugh. My face turns red, and a reddish-purple color. It feels like someone is pinching my neck. Breathing is very difficult. At the same time, I cough and spit up thick phlegm. Each episode lasts at least a week. (1) I don't know if I can ever get better (from the age of five to now). (2) Eating a little more food will trigger an episode. If I starve for a day, or eat something sour, it is lighter. I don't know what's going on. (3) Our doctor says it's asthma. Is that right? (4) What kind of medicine can I use to treat it? Can it be cured?

The name of your disease is "bronchial asthma." It is a disease of a special constitution. In the future, when injecting "serum," using "arsenic," "adrenal glands," and injecting "Salvarsan," you must pay special attention. The causes are "anemia," "weakness," "rhinitis," and "tonsillar hypertrophy." I don't know if you have these diseases. If you do, you must treat them first before you can talk about treating this disease. (1) If this disease can be cured at your age, it may never recur for the rest of your life. Otherwise, it may become a lifelong illness. (2) Overeating is a trigger for this disease. Sour foods have a curative effect on this disease. (3) Yes. (4) "Ephedrine" can be used, one tablet three times a day, every six hours, it is effective. Other drugs such as "Pacdin" and "Kresocal" can be taken. Whether it can be completely cured is not a matter of medicine, but a matter of hygiene. That is, whether the underlying disease can be cured, whether attention can be paid to warmth and cold, whether the diet can be careful, and whether the environment can be changed.

Abdominal Pain After Meals

No. 4 Mr. Yu Jia asks: (1) One or two hours after meals, I have pain above my navel, like burning and stabbing. Is this a stomach problem or an intestinal problem? (2) What about taking "Wei Bao?" (3) My stool is black. I don't know if it is related to drinking strong tea? (4) What medicine is suitable for treatment? (5) Can you treat this disease? (6) Is it dangerous?

(1) It is a stomach problem. It is a "stomach ulcer!" (2) I don't dare to comment because I don't know the ingredients of this medicine. (3) No. It is latent bleeding, which is also a symptom of stomach ulcers. (4) You can take "Biscama," but medication is only part of the treatment. Sanitary treatment should be paid attention to at the same time. (5) Yes. (6) It is not dangerous to life, but it is difficult to cure.

Poor Memory

No. 5 Mr. Zhang Yi asks: I have been poor since I was a child and have been studying hard. At the age of seventeen, I already had symptoms of poor memory. I often forgot things. I often couldn't remember where I put things. I searched everywhere, but the result was still in my hand. I can't understand what I read, especially foreign languages. It's very difficult. I like to fantasize. What I think about is mostly useless to me, but I can't stop myself. When I'm reading, I haven't even read half a page before my mind has already wandered off. I also dream a lot, and nightmares come frequently. When I wake up, I don't know where I've been. Please tell me: (1) Is this neurasthenia? (2) I like to read medical books, and the more I read, the more it seems like my own illness. My heart is burning like fire. (3) I have taken countless medicines before, but none of them have been effective. Please tell me a medicine that I can take regularly.

(1) Yes. (2) This is the worst phenomenon. It is best to abandon these kinds of books and never recall the words in them again. You should also not dwell on your own illness. You must know that this disease is not incurable. (3) You can regularly take "Hormspermin." Many so-called brain tonics on the market contain drugs. Not only are they ineffective, but they are also harmful. Medication is in the last place for this disease. The most important thing is to change the environment and abandon academic competition. In my opinion, there is very little connection between career prospects and reading books. Even if you finish reading a book and remember it all in your mind, the knowledge is only limited to this book. How far is the book from practical application? It goes without saying that even if it matches the facts, how much of it is actually used? I have seen bookworms who can't say a word to guests. I have seen those who have read "Arabian Nights" and cannot say a word to Westerners, or those who read a section of the mainland newspaper. In my opinion, if you are studying social sciences, you should experience life and replace psychology and sociology. If you are studying natural sciences, you should pay attention to practice. The foundation of science is in practice. Reading more books is useless.

I've said too much. I'm getting further and further away from the topic. I'll stop here. If you have any more questions, send a letter or talk face to face. I am willing to guide you to the best of my knowledge.

Is She Pregnant?

No. 6 Mrs. Feng Xueyuru asks: I have been married to my husband since last year. Until three months ago, my menstruation suddenly stopped. I often feel dizzy, my limbs are weak, and I like to eat sour things, but I don't feel their taste. (1) Please tell me, am I pregnant? (2) How should I take care of myself? (3) Or is it a disease?

Madam, this question is outside of the limitations of this doctor (this is an obstetrical question, and I am limited to internal medicine, dermatology, and venereology). This time, I will make an exception to answer, but there will be no more exceptions: (1) The symptoms described are not definite signs of pregnancy. It cannot be determined whether you are pregnant. A reliable method is to test your urine (available at all doctors' offices, for a price of about twenty yuan). Furthermore, your menstruation has been stopped for three months. If you are pregnant, after this time, the baby's heartbeat can be heard in your abdomen. (2) There are many things that should be taken care of. Due to limited space, I cannot answer them one by one. After confirming, consult a specialist doctor. (3) If the diagnostic method in (1) is negative, then it is a disease.

Is It Syphilis?

No. 7 Mr. Sun Zhan'ao asks: I was tempted by bad friends and went in and out of houses where women sell laughter every day. This spring, I contracted gonorrhea and a fleshy cylinder grew on the bottom end of my penis. I was diagnosed and treated and fully recovered. After that, I tested my blood and there was no syphilis. However, recently, I have been suffering from dizziness, headaches, back pain, weakness in my limbs, sore throat, body aches, and red spots on my chest, but they disappeared without treatment. (1) Please tell me, what is this disease? (2) What method should I use to treat it? (3) How much will it cost?

(1) There is a great suspicion of syphilis. One blood test without toxins is not entirely reliable, because in the early stages of induration, the blood test is often negative. To resolve the doubts, it is best to test again (note that tests performed within one month after injection to treat syphilis are also unreliable). (2) If it is syphilis, then anti-syphilitic therapy should be used. Inject "Arsphenamine" up to five centimeters (at the same time, inject "Bismuth for Syphilis" (Bismudol) or "Carbisin" until it reaches five centimeters, then stop for one month, and then test the blood again. If it is positive, further treatment is required. If it is negative, it is still not enough to represent a complete cure. It is advisable to test the blood again after half a year. (3) Each doctor has different diagnostic practices, which are different.

Discussion

Please Enlarge Chairman Han's Vision a Bit

— Me

According to a Jinan telegram, Shandong is cracking down on strange and outlandish clothing, implementing it strictly. One day, Han Fuju personally caught three women wearing strange and outlandish clothing. The Public Security Bureau also continued to arrest more than fifty people, all of whom were sent to the military court to await trial. It is said that women wearing strange and outlandish clothing parade through the streets, tempting young men, which can indeed be banned. Moreover, Chairman Han has issued repeated orders banning women from wearing strange and outlandish clothing, strictly prohibiting it. However, there are still women wearing strange and outlandish clothing who parade through the streets, disregarding the law. They were caught by Chairman Han himself. It is clear that these women deserved their fate.

However, women like to be pretty, like to be beautiful, and like to be fashionable. This is a common trait of women. Therefore, these women wearing strange and outlandish clothing who parade through the streets, although they are not as good as women who have read "Rules for the Women's Quarters" and "Daughter's Classic," who only knew the three obediences and four virtues, they are not committing any illegal acts in the modern trend. Because the current trend is too far away from the era of "banning different words and punishing different clothes."

Moreover, the so-called women wearing strange and outlandish clothing nowadays all come from Europeanization. However, Chinese women are not ambitious. They don't learn the spirit of European women, but only learn the superficial aspects of European women. Even more, they are not ambitious and become the wives and children of our weak country's citizens, instead of becoming the wives and children of citizens of rich and powerful European and American countries. As a result, they are regarded by the authorities as妖孽,魔障, and destroyers of good customs. All the unfortunate events in the country are often blamed on women wearing strange and outlandish clothing. It is truly unfair.

However, I do not hold such a view. I believe that these women wearing strange and outlandish clothing should go to court and should suffer. Regardless of their strange and outlandish clothing, even though it does not violate any criminal penalties under the current laws of the National Government, they should try the flavor of prison, because the laws of a local authority are no different from the laws of the country. People living in that area should have an obligation to obey the laws of the local authority. Chairman Han has issued a ban in the past, but the women in that area are unwilling to comply. Not only do they wear strange and outlandish clothing at home, but they dare to wear strange and outlandish clothing and parade through the streets. They should be as serious as 共黨盗贼 and be judged by a military judge.

A provincial governor bears the heavy responsibility of a province and should be well aware of the overall situation. He does not need to nitpick. If he grabs women on the road and interferes with their clothing in the market, this is not the behavior of a provincial chairman, but something that ordinary clerks do. Shandong Province has an extremely difficult problem in front of it, which is also a matter of life and death for Shandong Province. Chairman Han must face it with a spirit of waiting for battle. The responsibility of a local official is so great. The most important ones are the responsibility to defend the country, the responsibility to defend the territory, and the responsibility to protect the people and secure their lives. Chairman Han should not easily let go of this kind of place. He should deal with it with a spirit of unyielding, uncompromising, non-compliance, and non-cooperation. Only then can he be called a pillar of the country and a backbone of the country. As for the clothing of women, it is not necessary to trouble the chairman's precious hands or worry the chairman's spirit. The so-called豺狼当道，安问狐狸 (when jackals are in power, why ask about foxes). If you only ask about foxes and not about jackals, this is called prioritizing what is light and lightening what is heavy. If Chairman Han really understands this meaning, then he may not have time for this kind of cautious thing.
